**Key features:**


------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Decentralized Platform:** Operates without a central owner, operator, or regulator
    
*   **Gaming revolution:** Immutable rules and 100% transparency powered by smart-contracts
    
*   **Staking:** Stake BET tokens to become a casino owner and earn on winning fees and lost bets

# Partners Intro | FOR PARTNERS | BETFIN DOCS

Become a Partner.

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/for-partners#video-transcript-vision-of-partnership)

Video Transcript - Vision of Partnership


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

_Betfin's vision would not be that revolutionary without the option to duplicate the platform as a white label solution. Yes, the partner contract gives you the opportunity to launch your Betfin clone with just a single click and a one-time license fee._

_Simply choose your tariff on the Partner page, sign the license with your secured wallet and your lifetime partner contract will be deployed within a few seconds!_

_What is great? Once you have a partner's contract you can connect it to your new or an already existing website or even connect it to a hardware device such as a slot machine!_

_What is better? Partners' games remain connected to the platform core contract so you generate profit from bets but all the payouts and also risk remain on the Betfin and staking users in any platform of the Betfin network!_

_What is the best? As a Betfin partner, you still generate the rewards for affiliation of staking and betting. Moreover, you can utilize the power of the affiliate to drive your team to build a network on your platform._

_That makes the Betfin platform the easiest gaming business ever. Learn more in the academy and become a Betfin Partner!_

[NextPartner Contract Explained](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/for-partners/about-partner-contract/partner-contract-explained)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Partner Contract Explained | FOR PARTNERS | BETFIN DOCS

![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1781694540-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FghcvsowmAIHcsfYLkJpA%252Fuploads%252FEIxXHY4t1kwfiQRdSvhs%252FScreenshot%25202024-03-10%2520at%252020.10.54.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D52d0362e-b057-484e-8acf-0c3e69a1d10b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f471e0d9&sv=2)

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/for-partners/about-partner-contract/partner-contract-explained#partner-principle)

Partner principle


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   In comparison to affiliate program which means only recommendation of user to BetFin ecosystem, Partner contract provides all transactions between a user and Betfin platform.
    
    *   That means all the members transactions has to go through Partner contract to access the BetFin ecosystem.
        
    
*   It is not possible to bet or stake without being delivered to the platform by a partner (and without [Betfin Pass NFT](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-explanation/betfin-pass-nft)
    ).
    
*   _**Partner contract is something that has all benefits of whitelabel solution and license agreement all at once**_
    

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/for-partners/about-partner-contract/partner-contract-explained#how-the-business-works)

How the business works


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Partners renumeration depends on [Partner Tariff Terms](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/for-partners/faq-and-terms/partner-tariff-terms)
     and volume generated in Staking and Betting of users partners brought to the platform via his UI.
    
    *   Renumeration is paid directly from or from winning fees in shared betting games.
        
    
*   Partner contract can be connected to any user interface.
    
    *   That gives the partner opportunity to build custom or copy Betfin UI with own branding
        
    *   It is also possible to connect the input to a device
        
    
*   The goal of the partner is to create a users friendly access point to the Betfin blockchain platform
    
    *   The vision is that the better UI will generate better volume and profit.
        
    *   Betfin does not insist on brand and moreover have not control of Partners brand
        
    *   Betfin.io website is example of how the UI may look like
        
    
*   Betfin community also provides a solution of UI whitelabel where you can use the BetFin.io clone ui.
    
    *   If you want to use the Betfin brand just for a local market, contact magnum@betfin.io
        
    

[PreviousPartners Intro](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/for-partners)
[NextSecurity Aspects](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/for-partners/about-partner-contract/security-aspects)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Partner Onboarding | FOR PARTNERS | BETFIN DOCS

The general onboarding process is the following:

1.  Purchase a partner contract with a single click.
    
2.  Purchase a domain.
    
3.  Translate words (Betfin community members will support you with source files after the partner contract is purchased).
    
4.  Create your brand or cooperate with the Betfin brand. Contact Betfin for brand cooperation while the contract is purchased.
    
5.  Create your UI updates (if applicable - custom brand).
    
6.  Connect the Betfin contract to the custom domain and frontend.
    
7.  Setup your marketing strategy and social media.
    
8.  Launch your partner contract to the public.
    

For Betfin team support contact us on magnum@betfin.io

[PreviousPartner Tariff Terms](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/for-partners/faq-and-terms/partner-tariff-terms)
[NextBrand Manual](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/for-partners/brand-manual)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Legal Aspects | FOR PARTNERS | BETFIN DOCS

Even if Betfin is decentralized, becoming a partner contract owner may bring certain consequences in certain jurisdictions. We always recommend considering such consequences before proceeding with a partner contract purchase and before marketing promotion. We recommend to discuss with your legal and tax advisor (at least) the following topics:

1.  Who should be the owner of the partner contract? Physical or natural person and in which country should it be based?
    
2.  Can you target your desired market directly with all the products? Would it help to hide some products on the front end?
    
3.  How can you promote it? Check the wording of the website and presentation materials.
    
4.  How the income from the partner contract will be swapped (if ever) to FIAT money?
    
5.  What are the tax impacts and how to do accounting properly?
    

Shall you need any asistance contact betfin on info@betfin.io or via telegram

[PreviousSecurity Aspects](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/for-partners/about-partner-contract/security-aspects)
[NextPartners FAQ](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/for-partners/faq-and-terms/partners-faq)

Last updated 11 months ago

# Security Aspects | FOR PARTNERS | BETFIN DOCS

allows youPartner contract is fully audited and secured already when deployed. However, the critical part of business operational security is the partner's OPSEC (operation security). If you own a partner contract and your wallet private key is leaked your earnings might be stolen each time you generate it. In such cases partner contract becomes worthless.

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/for-partners/about-partner-contract/security-aspects#purchase-trezor-or-ledger-hardware-wallet)

**Purchase Trezor or Ledger Hardware Wallet**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Always purchase the hardware wallet from a certified reseller in your local market
    

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/for-partners/about-partner-contract/security-aspects#use-a-proper-way-of-seed-backup)

**Use a Proper Way of Seed Backup**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   We recommend metallic tabs and engraving the seeds on it.
    
*   Use Shamir backup seed instead of classical seed phrase.
    
    *   That gives you an opportunity to distribute seed in more than one location.
        
    *   Read here: [https://trezor.io/learn/a/what-is-shamir-backup](https://trezor.io/learn/a/what-is-shamir-backup)
        
    
*   We recommend Shamir 2/3 or 3/5.
    
*   Never make any digital backup on any device.
    
*   Prepare a backup device in case of loss or damage.
    
    *   It might be hard to restore your device, but we recommend having at least one backup device that is well-stored.
        
    
*   Protect your hardware wallet with a strong pin.
    
    *   We recommend at least 6 digits for operational and 10 digits for backup device.
        
    *   Don't make it easy to guess.
        
    

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/for-partners/about-partner-contract/security-aspects#use-a-multisig-wallet)

**Use a Multisig Wallet**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   We recommend using [**safe.globa**l](https://safe.global/)
     multisig contract that can be an owner of the Partner contract.
    
*   That allows you to sell the partner contract in case you decide or transfer its ownership.
    
*   This protects you from a physical attack from the contract owner.
    
*   We recommend a 2/3 quorum.
    

[PreviousPartner Contract Explained](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/for-partners/about-partner-contract/partner-contract-explained)
[NextLegal Aspects](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/for-partners/about-partner-contract/legal-aspects)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Partners FAQ | FOR PARTNERS | BETFIN DOCS

What does it mean to be a Betfin partner?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/for-partners/faq-and-terms/partners-faq#what-does-it-mean-to-be-a-betfin-partner)

That means to own a Partner contract which gives you an opportunity to utilise the full business potential of the Betfin platform without undertaking any risk. That means that you can bring users to the Betfin platform through our or your own interface (your brand) and at the same time use all the Betfin technology as it is yours. You can still participate in the Betfin affiliate.

How can I become a partner?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/for-partners/faq-and-terms/partners-faq#how-can-i-become-a-partner)

You visit our page betfin.io/partner, choose the desired partner tariff and simply deploy the contract by paying the onetime license fee.

How does the partner contract work?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/for-partners/faq-and-terms/partners-faq#how-does-the-partner-contract-work)

Partner has a special contract that works as a variable symbol of the bet to recognise that the user placed a bet via Partner's license.

Check out more about the technical functions here [Partner Contract Explained](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/for-partners/about-partner-contract/partner-contract-explained)
.

How much does the partner Earn?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/for-partners/faq-and-terms/partners-faq#how-much-does-the-partner-earn)

Check out our Partners' conditions here [Partner Tariff Terms](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/for-partners/faq-and-terms/partner-tariff-terms)
.

Your income is not limited.

Who pays the partner?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/for-partners/faq-and-terms/partners-faq#who-pays-the-partner)

In case of sharebets such as Predict the partner is paid directly from the winning fee. In case of any staking or Lotto games such as Roulette, partners are paid from the partner reserve pool.

Is affiliate applied also to Partners contracts?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/for-partners/faq-and-terms/partners-faq#is-affiliate-applied-also-to-partners-contracts)

Yes, affiliate works completely the same for partners websites. This is why Partners are usually also active in affiliate system to maximize their rewards.

Is there any limitation of partner contract?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/for-partners/faq-and-terms/partners-faq#is-there-any-limitation-of-partner-contract)

No, there is no limit for time or teritorry.

Can I create my own domain and brand?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/for-partners/faq-and-terms/partners-faq#can-i-create-my-own-domain-and-brand)

Yes, you can operate under any domain or brand you wish. We recommend to connect your partner contract to our evidence in order to be officialy mentioned in Betfin's official media.

Is affiliate applied also to Partners contracts?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/for-partners/faq-and-terms/partners-faq#is-affiliate-applied-also-to-partners-contracts-1)

Yes, affiliate works completely the same for partners websites. This is why Partners are usually also active in affiliate system.

[PreviousLegal Aspects](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/for-partners/about-partner-contract/legal-aspects)
[NextPartner Tariff Terms](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/for-partners/faq-and-terms/partner-tariff-terms)

# Partner Tariff Terms | FOR PARTNERS | BETFIN DOCS

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/for-partners/faq-and-terms/partner-tariff-terms#terms)

TERMS


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   The tariff price is a one-time setup fee you paid to the CORE contract.
    
*   Betfin may change the partner tariff conditions at any time without any prior notice.
    
    *   Betfin is not obliged to announce tariff changes publicly but all changes are public records in the blockchain.
        
    
*   Partner is not able to upgrade from one tariff to another.
    
    *   A new tariff has to be purchased if you want to change terms.
        
    
*   Betfin can not block or blacklist the partner contract. It is technically impossible.
    
*   Partners can use the Betfin brand or their own brand.
    
*   Anyone except the partner contract owner can claim the revenues from the contract.
    
*   Partner contract is non-transferable to any other owner but can be owned by multisig contract in which ownership can be transferred.
    
*   You can not finish the contract - if you wish to stop, then block the UI that would allow your users to access the Betfin platform.
    
*   There is no limit for time or territory in terms of the technical solution.
    

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/for-partners/faq-and-terms/partner-tariff-terms#conditions)

CONDITIONS


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**NOTES:**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   By purchasing a license you are increasing the [Partners Pool](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/tokenomy/bet-initial-distribution/partners-pool)
    which is held by [Core](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/core)
     contract
    
*   Partner is being paid out of the winning fees in case of conservative games and from contract ( which holds the Partner pool reserve) in case of any staking or lotto games.
    
*   Games and staking remuneration means percentage share per volume produced. Users' revenue or bet result has no impact on the partner.
    
*   Partner holds no financial responsibility for users' winnings, staking payout etc.
    
*   Partner does not have to proceed with any steps to execute bets or staking payout.

# Welcome to Betfin Staking | STAKING MANUAL | BETFIN DOCS

Betfin staking intro

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual#conservative-staking)

**Conservative Staking**

A low-risk option allowing users stake their tokens in pools with predetermined terms and conditions. This type of staking offers predictable and stable returns over time.

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual#dynamic-staking)

**Dynamic Staking**

A higher-risk, higher-reward option where the staking conditions and returns can fluctuate based on the pool's performance and other factors.

[https://firebasestorage.googleapis.com/v0/b/betfin-dev.appspot.com/o/Betfin\_Stake%20and%20Earn.mp4?alt=media&token=9c1cab12-0c33-429a-8de4-e29767f29a2afirebasestorage.googleapis.com](https://firebasestorage.googleapis.com/v0/b/betfin-dev.appspot.com/o/Betfin_Stake%20and%20Earn.mp4?alt=media&token=9c1cab12-0c33-429a-8de4-e29767f29a2a)

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual#benefits-of-staking-at-betfin)

Benefits of Staking at Betfin

1.  **Great returns** \- long term profit backed by mathematical advantage
    
2.  **Enhanced Security:** Your investment is as secured as your wallet private key, there is no third party that affects security of the contract.
    
3.  **Flexibility:** You can choose between conservative and dynamic staking depending on your investment strategy.
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual#getting-started-with-staking)

Getting Started with Staking

1.  **Connect Wallet:** Ensure your wallet is connected to the Betfin platform.
    
2.  **Choose Staking Type:** Select either conservative or dynamic staking based on your preference.
    
3.  **Stake Tokens:** Follow the instructions to stake your BET tokens in the pool of your preference.
    

For detailed guidelines and terms, explore the specific sections for [Conservative Staking](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual#conservative-staking)
 and [Dynamic Staking](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual#dynamic-staking)
 manual. Happy staking with Betfin!

[NextConservative Staking Manual](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-user-manual/conservative-staking-manual)

Last updated 11 months ago

# Brand Manual | FOR PARTNERS | BETFIN DOCS

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/for-partners/brand-manual#brand-guidelines)

Brand Guidelines


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Betfin.io is a decentralized gaming platform that connects players and stakers in a single ecosystem. Players can not only place bets and enjoy fair blockchain-powered games but also stake their funds and share in the platform’s profits. Likewise, stakers can invest and generate passive income while also participating in the games themselves.

Thanks to smart contracts, all transactions are secure, instant, and transparent. Stakers provide liquidity to the platform, ensuring its smooth operation, while also having the opportunity to play and benefit from decentralized gaming.

Our core values:

*   Decentralization – Full control over funds for both players and stakers.
    
*   Transparency – Blockchain ensures transparency and fair gameplay.
    
*   Fairness – Random winnings are generated by Chainlink VRF and Gelato.
    

Betfin.io is more than just a casino – it’s a revolutionary platform where the line between player and staker disappears, allowing everyone to do both.

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/for-partners/brand-manual#tone-of-communication)

Tone of Communication


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Language**

Friendly yet professional. Use language that reflects the technological nature of DeFi while remaining accessible to a broader audience.

Incorporate terms like "blockchain technology," "DeFi," and "smart contracts" to communicate technological advantages.

**Tone of communication**

Motivational and energetic – Emphasize the benefits of decentralized gaming.

Transparent and trustworthy – Highlight how blockchain ensures transparency and security.

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/for-partners/brand-manual#logo-variants)

# Conservative Staking Manual | STAKING MANUAL | BETFIN DOCS

![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1670244672-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FC2OFugUqsqIbeojX8DmZ%252Fuploads%252Fbq9k0s40x5IGgQTnR75b%252FScreenshot%25202024-03-10%2520at%252020.07.41.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6208df96-edde-49d3-a6a0-dfdf35bf22d7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b3b2963e&sv=2)

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-user-manual/conservative-staking-manual#staking-process)

**Staking Process:**

1.  **Connect Wallet:**
    
    *   Connect your wallet to the Betfin platform.
        
    *   _**See the**_
        
    
2.  **Select Conservative Staking:**
    
    *   Choose the "Conservative Staking" option from the staking menu.
        
    
3.  **Enter Stake Amount:**
    
    *   Input the amount of BET tokens you wish to stake.
        
    
    ![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1670244672-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FC2OFugUqsqIbeojX8DmZ%252Fuploads%252FzeyhmmNjgCSHyAW3YeOR%252FScreenshot%25202024-04-28%2520at%252013.13.49.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D340f6351-faba-4ec5-b5ea-e0b533a77e42&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ca86f8a6&sv=2)
    
    This is how that staking execution window looks like. Make sure you are in Conservative staking page.
    
4.  **Confirm Transaction:**
    
    *   Confirm the transaction in your wallet to complete the staking process.
        
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-user-manual/conservative-staking-manual#key-tips)

**Key Tips:**

*   **Early Staking Advantage:**
    
    *   Staking early ensures your position in a pool, starting the 80-week countdown from the pool's creation.
        
    *   Multiple stakes within the same pool are combined to the same position for convenience and optimization.
        
    
*   **Regular Staking:**
    
    *   Regular staking helps manage liquidity and optimize profits through consistent participation.
        
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-user-manual/conservative-staking-manual#benefits-of-conservative-staking)

**Benefits of Conservative Staking:**

*   **No Risk of Token Loss:**
    
    *   Tokens are safely staked with transparent rules.
        
    
*   **Earnings from Fees:**
    
    *   Earn a portion of the fees generated from Betfin's conservative games.
        
    
*   **Predictable Returns:**
    
    *   Enjoy consistent and predictable staking rewards.
        
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-user-manual/conservative-staking-manual#managing-your-stake)

**Managing Your Stake:**

*   **Monitor Your Stake:**
    
    *   Track your staking progress and rewards through the Betfin dashboard.
        
    
*   **Claim Rewards:**
    
    *   Periodically claim your staking rewards to maximize your earnings.
        
    

![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1670244672-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FC2OFugUqsqIbeojX8DmZ%252Fuploads%252FA2uyRxDdoCySqwrUcQmc%252FScreenshot%25202024-04-28%2520at%252013.38.26.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db84544e8-ecea-490f-8546-90eaf87ea685&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=28917185&sv=2)

This is how the claim balance should look like.

*   **Restake or Unstake:**
    
    *   At the end of each 80-week cycle, decide whether to restake or unstake your tokens for flexibility and continued earning potential without any further lockup period.
        
    

![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1670244672-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FC2OFugUqsqIbeojX8DmZ%252Fuploads%252Fg6yI4AVgZqk6THmoSVK7%252FScreenshot%25202024-04-28%2520at%252013.17.39.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ded79fa03-c6c8-469f-9819-2732e3981fb8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c7176730&sv=2)

My staking page

# Example of conservative staking | STAKING MANUAL | BETFIN DOCS

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-user-manual/conservative-staking-manual/example-of-conservative-staking#inputs)

Inputs


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   There are 2 staking members A & B:
    
    *   A stakes 4,000 BET
        
    *   B stakes 6,000 BET
        
    
*   There is a 3,6% fee for all possible winnings:
    
    *   Let's assume there is no partner that should receive a share of this volume
        
    *   The partner that operates the platform charges 0% (maximal possible tariff is 1,2% = 1/3 of winning fees)
        
    
*   There was a total winning volume of 100,000 BET in shared bets in 1st cycle.
    

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-user-manual/conservative-staking-manual/example-of-conservative-staking#profit-calculation)

Profit calculation


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   That equals 3,600 BET tokens that go to conservative staking.
    
*   Those 3,6k shall be distributed proportionally among users A & B according to their staking volume.
    
*   The ratio between staking members A:B is 4,000:6,000
    
    *   User A receives 4,000 shares of the 3,6k payout = 1,440 BET
        
    *   User B receives 6,000 shares of the 3,6k payout = 2,160 BET
        
    

![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1670244672-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FC2OFugUqsqIbeojX8DmZ%252Fuploads%252FSqnA10RZA5qjR9TMMp60%252FScreenshot%25202024-05-12%2520at%252014.22.39.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D14d68c7a-195e-4a3c-9acd-0525ebeb7bdd&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5da387c3&sv=2)

**Distribution of rewards in conservative staking.**

*   As there is no possibility of receiving a negative result we can say that all cycles will look similar.
    
*   This example is a simplified business logic explanation that does not include the internal accounting that is described in [Conservative Pool Accounting](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/conservative-pool-accounting)
    .
    

[PreviousConservative Staking Manual](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-user-manual/conservative-staking-manual)
[NextDynamic Staking Manual](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-user-manual/dynamic-staking-manual)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Dynamic Staking Example | STAKING MANUAL | BETFIN DOCS

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-user-manual/dynamic-staking-manual/dynamic-staking-example#inputs)

Inputs


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   There are 2 staking members A & B:
    
    *   A stakes 4,000 BET.
        
    *   B stakes 6,000 BET.
        
    *   Both users stake in the same cycle to the same pool.
        
    
*   There was a total volume of 100,000 bets in dynamic games that generated a profit of 3,600 BET.
    

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-user-manual/dynamic-staking-manual/dynamic-staking-example#profit-calculation)

Profit Calculation


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   There is no drawdown in the pool as it is the first pool ever.
    
*   An amount of 3,600 BET is distributed to the pool.
    
*   Pool distributes the 3,600 BET in proportion:
    
    *   Payout to user A is 1,440 BET
        
    *   Payout to user B is 2,160 BET
        
    

[PreviousDynamic Staking Manual](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-user-manual/dynamic-staking-manual)
[NextConservative Staking Terms](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-terms/conservative-staking-terms)

# Conservative Staking Terms | STAKING MANUAL | BETFIN DOCS

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-terms/conservative-staking-terms#changeable-conservative-staking-constants)

Changeable Conservative Staking Constants


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

_**Conservative staking limits are possible to change in the contract following the pre-defined conditions.**_

Current limits

Maximal possible limits

Those are the currently valid limits that are set as the best for the BetFin community growth.

Settings name

Current settings

Explanation

Minimal staking size

10,000 BET

10,000 BET

Maximal staking size

N/A

There is no limit

Calculation window length

300 sec

5 minutes (Friday 12 AM UTC)

This table describes maximal and minimal limits that can be set by the administrator's quorum for each constant of settings.

Settings name

Lowes limit

Highest limit

Minimal staking size (1 stake)

3 000 BET

10,000,000 BET

Maximal staking size

There is no limit

There is no limit

Calculation window length

300 sec

24 hours

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-terms/conservative-staking-terms#conservative-staking-hardcoded-terms)

**Conservative Staking Hardcoded Terms**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Following conservative staking terms are hardcoded so they can not be changed under any circumstances.**

Settings name

Current settings

Explanation

Length of 1 cycle

604,800 sec

1 week (since Friday 12 AM UTC)

Staking duration

80 cycles

80 weeks since staked

Staking start

Immediate

Staking starts immediately when created

Eligibility for payout

Immediately

You get your first cycle payout the first Friday after stake. There is no impact on payout based on which day you stake

Unlock right / obligation

none except duration

*   Unlock is possible only after staking ends
    
*   After staking ends the unlock is not mandatory
    
*   Staking earns rewards even after its duration ends
    

Unlock process

Each stake single

Each stake is unlocked independently from other stakes. Each stake has to be unlocked separately by its owner.

Stakes in one pool

100

After the pool is filled a new pool is created

Unfilled pool over cycle

continues

Not filled pools continue in the next cycle without effect

**Looking for other terms? Visit**

[PreviousDynamic Staking Example](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-user-manual/dynamic-staking-manual/dynamic-staking-example)
[NextDynamic Staking Terms](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-terms/dynamic-staking-terms)

# Dynamic Staking Manual | STAKING MANUAL | BETFIN DOCS

![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1670244672-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FC2OFugUqsqIbeojX8DmZ%252Fuploads%252Fbq9k0s40x5IGgQTnR75b%252FScreenshot%25202024-03-10%2520at%252020.07.41.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6208df96-edde-49d3-a6a0-dfdf35bf22d7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b3b2963e&sv=2)

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-user-manual/dynamic-staking-manual#steps-to-stake)

Steps to Stake:

1.  **Verify Betfin Pass**: Ensure you have a Betfin pass in your wallet.
    
2.  **Stake BET Tokens**:
    
    *   Connect your wallet.
        
    *   Navigate to the dynamic staking section.
        
    *   Enter the amount you wish to stake (must meet the minimum requirements set by the terms).
        
    *   Confirm and lock your tokens for the staking period.
        
    
3.  **Rewards**:
    
    *   Rewards are distributed at the end of each staking cycle.
        
    *   The rewards distribution happens once for all participants, and you do not need to claim them individually.
        
    
4.  **Duration**: Stakes are locked for 20 cycles, with each cycle lasting 4 weeks, from Monday to Monday at 12:00 UTC.
    
5.  **Increasing Stakes**: If the results are negative, consider increasing your stakes to have a larger share compared to others.
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-user-manual/dynamic-staking-manual#tips)

Tips:

*   **Risk Awareness**: Be aware that there is a risk of losing tokens. One unlucky spin can reduce the dynamic pool by up to 5%.
    
*   **Staking Strategy**: Regularly increase your stakes, especially after negative rounds, to maintain a favourable position in the staking pool.
    
*   **Reward Distribution**: Understand that the profit-sharing process involves distributing rewards proportionally to all stakers.
    

For more detailed accounting information, refer to the [Dynamic Pool Accounting](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/dynamic-pool-accounting)

[PreviousExample of conservative staking](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-user-manual/conservative-staking-manual/example-of-conservative-staking)
[NextDynamic Staking Example](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-user-manual/dynamic-staking-manual/dynamic-staking-example)

Hardcoded dynamic staking terms


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Following dynamic staking terms are hardcoded and can not be changed under any circumstances.**

Settings name

Current settings

Explanation

Length of 1 cycle

604,800 sec

4 weeks (since Monday 12 AM UTC)

Staking duration

20 cycles + pool closing

80 weeks since pool is closed

Staking start

Pool closing time

*   Staking duration starts after the dynamic staking pool is closed
    
*   If you stake more than once in one cycle then all your stakes will be counted in the first pool you staked in.
    

Closing pool condition

End of cycle or full pool

The dynamic staking pool is closed once the pool is full (100 stakes) or once the cycle ends (once per 4 weeks)

Eligibility for payout

Immediately

You get your first cycle payout once the first cycle ends

Unlock right / obligation

None except duration

*   Unlock is possible only after staking ends
    
*   After staking ends the unlock is not mandatory
    
*   Staking earns rewards even after its duration ends (including the negative staking results)
    

Unlock process

Whole pool unlock as a bulk

Once the staking duration ends any staking owner is eligible for unlock. This action unlocks and executes all stakes in the pool to the owner's staking balance.

Max pool capacity

100

Once the pool reaches 100 stakes it is closed and a new pool is opened

Unfilled pool over cycle

Closes

If the pool is not filled once the cycle ends it is closed. At the beginning of the new pool, there is always a new pool opened.

# Conservative Pool Accounting | STAKING MANUAL | BETFIN DOCS

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/conservative-pool-accounting#overview)

**Overview:**

Conservative staking on Betfin allows users to lock BET tokens in a secure, predictable environment, earning returns through platform fees and game profits.

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/conservative-pool-accounting#key-features)

**Key Features:**

*   **Fixed Duration:** Each staking pool operates on an 80-week cycle, starting from the pool's creation date.
    
*   **Predictable Returns:** Users earn staking rewards based on the performance of Betfin's conservative games.
    
*   **Pool Structure:** Tokens are divided into pools, each pool can hold up to 100 stakes. When a pool is full, a new pool is automatically created.
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/conservative-pool-accounting#how-it-works)

**How It Works:**

#### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/conservative-pool-accounting#staking-pools)

**Staking Pools**

*   Pools are created upon user demand and filled sequentially. Each pool starts a new 80-week cycle from its creation date.
    

![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1670244672-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FC2OFugUqsqIbeojX8DmZ%252Fuploads%252F6bCnoGUnehDwjSFdqWtD%252F7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3320efa8-5f74-4dca-92d2-27a23a4f1252&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b417dfe2&sv=2)

Illustrative image of conservative staking in pool.

*   The purpose of the conservative pool is that payout is being distributed among the pools instead of directly to the staking contracts and that is what gives the platform higher scalability.
    
*   There is not any difference in which pool is your stake (each 1 BET in 1 cycle generates the same payout without a difference in which pool it was staked).
    
*   Each pool is owned by the conservative staking contract which governs the profit distribution .
    

#### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/conservative-pool-accounting#reward-distribution)

**Reward Distribution**

*   **Non-negative Returns:** The yield can be either zero or positive, never negative.
    
*   **Profit Allocation:** Profits from conservative games are allocated to pools first. These pools then distribute the profits among individual stakes proportionally.
    

![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1670244672-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FC2OFugUqsqIbeojX8DmZ%252Fuploads%252FuPagkMOgAS3qeuwf4elV%252F9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D950c7a34-3cbe-4dcf-b1c2-44203fcbc837&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=11cf75d8&sv=2)

This is the distribution of revenues from the conservative staking among the conservative pools.

![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1670244672-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FC2OFugUqsqIbeojX8DmZ%252Fuploads%252FbIqTDF2Darsqw5lkm18e%252F10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D44c83711-871f-4c57-b733-4c8a869426c5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a4cc1759&sv=2)

This is distribution of revenues within the pool number 3 among 5 stakes that currently exist.

**Calculation Window:** This process occurs during the calculation window, a specific period at the end of each cycle when the pool's performance is evaluated, and rewards are calculated and distributed.

#### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/conservative-pool-accounting#end-of-cycle)

**End of Cycle:**

*   At the end of 80 weeks, users must decide whether to restake their tokens for another cycle or unstake to withdraw their tokens.
    
*   Users need to claim their rewards regularly during the staking period to maximize their earnings.
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/conservative-pool-accounting#benefits)

**Benefits:**

*   **No Token Loss:** Staked tokens remain safe and are returned after the staking period.
    
*   **Transparency:** All transactions and pool activities are recorded on the blockchain, ensuring transparency.
    
*   **Earnings from Fees:** Users earn a share of the platform's fees, providing a steady income stream.
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/conservative-pool-accounting#conclusion)

**Conclusion:**

Conservative staking offers a low-risk way to earn predictable returns by participating in the Betfin ecosystem. By understanding the pool structure and the importance of regular claims, users can maximize their staking rewards.

[PreviousStaking Pools & Scalability](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/staking-pools-and-scalability)
[NextDynamic Pool Accounting](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/dynamic-pool-accounting)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Dynamic Pool Accounting | STAKING MANUAL | BETFIN DOCS

Dynamic staking within the Betfin platform offers a flexible approach to staking, balancing both profits and drawdowns effectively. Here is an in-depth look at its accounting mechanics:

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/dynamic-pool-accounting#key-features)

**Key Features:**

*   **Flexible Duration:** Operates on adaptable cycles to match platform needs.
    
*   **Risk Management:** Caps drawdowns at 5% of the dynamic pool per round.
    
*   **Profit Calculation:** Considers both positive and negative results based on game performance.
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/dynamic-pool-accounting#staking-pools)

**Staking Pools:**

*   **Stake Limit:** Each pool can hold up to 100 stakes. New pools are created at the start of each cycle or when the stake limit is reached.
    
*   **Funds Balancing:** The main staking contract balances funds between dynamic staking sub-pools, ensuring efficient capital allocation and risk management.
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/dynamic-pool-accounting#profit-distribution)

**Profit Distribution:**

*   **From Dynamic Staking to Pools:** Profits generated from dynamic staking games are first allocated to dynamic staking pools.
    
*   **From Pools to Users:** The profits are then distributed from the pools proportionally among its stakers based on their contributions.
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/dynamic-pool-accounting#profit-distribution-scenarios)

**Profit Distribution Scenarios:**

**Positive profit, pool without drawdown**

1.  The system counts how big a share the specific pool has on the total profit.
    

1.  Payout is distributed to specific staking contracts.
    

**Negative profit, pool without drawdown**

1.  The system counts how big a share the specific pool has on the total lost.
    

1.  The total lost is assigned to the pool as a pool drawdown for the next period.
    

**Positive profit, pool with drawdown**

1.  The system counts how big a share the specific pool has on the total profit.
    

1.  If the pool profit is higher than the total drawdown from past cycles the remaining part of the payout is distributed to specific staking contracts.
    

1.  If the pool profit does not cover the drawdown the drawdown is only decreased for the appropriate sum.
    

**Negative profit, pool with drawdown**

1.  The system counts how big a share the specific pool has of total negative profit.
    

1.  The total drawdown is increased for the pool share on the total negative profit.
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/dynamic-pool-accounting#calculation-window)

**Calculation Window:**

*   **Performance Evaluation:** Occurs at the end of each cycle, evaluating pool performance to calculate and distribute rewards.
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/dynamic-pool-accounting#risk-mitigation)

**Risk Mitigation:**

*   **Controlled Drawdown:** Ensures no single round's drawdown exceeds 5% of the pool.
    
*   **Mechanism of decreasing loss:** Users can never reach 100% loss as the negative profit creates a lower base of each stake. That motivates new stakers and protects drawdowned stakers.
    
*   **Main pool vs sub-pools** - 50% of stakes being held on the staking pools and the remaining 50% being held directly on the staking contract.
    
    *   50% on dynamic staking contract gives players the coverage of winnings in dynamic games
        
    *   50% on dynamic staking pools is to cover potential loss in dynamic staking
        
    

Dynamic staking on Betfin offers a robust and flexible way for users to earn returns, leveraging the platform's gaming activities. Understanding the intricacies of profit distribution and risk management allows users to maximize their staking benefits while maintaining a clear perspective on potential risks.

[PreviousConservative Pool Accounting](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/conservative-pool-accounting)
[NextScenarios in Dynamic Staking](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/dynamic-pool-accounting/scenarios-in-dynamic-staking)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Scenarios in Dynamic Staking | STAKING MANUAL | BETFIN DOCS

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/dynamic-pool-accounting/scenarios-in-dynamic-staking#scenarios-related-to-profits-and-losses)

**Scenarios Related to Profits and Losses:**

#### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/dynamic-pool-accounting/scenarios-in-dynamic-staking#profitable-cycle)

**Profitable Cycle**

*   **Description:** At the end of the cycle, the total profit is calculated.
    
*   **Fund Allocation:** Profits are distributed from the main contract to sub-pools and then to individual stakers based on their stake amount minus any drawdowns.
    

#### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/dynamic-pool-accounting/scenarios-in-dynamic-staking#negative-cycle)

**Negative Cycle**

*   **Description:** At the end of the cycle, the total loss (drawdown) is calculated.
    
*   **Fund Allocation:** Losses are recorded against sub-pools. Future profits first cover these drawdowns before any distribution to stakers.
    

#### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/dynamic-pool-accounting/scenarios-in-dynamic-staking#partial-pool-profit-loss)

**Partial Pool Profit/Loss**

*   **Description:** Some sub-pools experience profit, while others experience a loss.
    
*   **Fund Allocation:** Profitable sub-pools distribute gains to users, while losses are covered by future profits. Drawdowns are managed at the sub-pool level.
    

#### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/dynamic-pool-accounting/scenarios-in-dynamic-staking#emergency-balancing)

**Emergency Balancing**

*   **Description:** Unexpected events cause an imbalance.
    
*   **Fund Allocation:** Funds are re-balanced across sub-pools to protect against excessive drawdowns and ensure liquidity.
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/dynamic-pool-accounting/scenarios-in-dynamic-staking#scenarios-related-to-the-end-of-stakes)

**Scenarios Related to the End of Stakes:**

#### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/dynamic-pool-accounting/scenarios-in-dynamic-staking#cycle-end-balancing)

**Cycle End Balancing**

*   **Description:** Re-balancing of funds across sub-pools at the end of a cycle.
    
*   **Fund Allocation:** Ensures stability by redistributing funds, covering drawdowns, and maintaining liquidity for the next cycle.
    

#### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/dynamic-pool-accounting/scenarios-in-dynamic-staking#stake-end)

**Stake End**

*   **Description:** Users' stakes reach the end of their 20-cycle duration.
    
*   **Fund Allocation:** Users must decide to either re-stake their tokens for another cycle or withdraw their tokens. Profits are distributed based on the performance of the sub-pool during the staking period.
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/dynamic-pool-accounting/scenarios-in-dynamic-staking#scenarios-related-to-new-stakes)

**Scenarios Related to New Stakes:**

#### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/dynamic-pool-accounting/scenarios-in-dynamic-staking#initial-staking)

**Initial Staking**

*   **Description:** Users stake tokens in the dynamic staking contract.
    
*   **Fund Allocation:** Stakes are assigned to relevant sub-pools based on capacity and cycle timing. Each pool has a fixed duration of 20 cycles (4 weeks each).
    

#### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/dynamic-pool-accounting/scenarios-in-dynamic-staking#adjusting-stakes-during-cycle)

**Adjusting Stakes During Cycle**

*   **Description:** Users adjust their stakes in sub-pools during an ongoing cycle.
    
*   **Fund Allocation:** New stakes are added to the relevant sub-pools, and withdrawals are managed to ensure stability. Adjustments are reflected in the next cycle.
    

* * *

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/dynamic-pool-accounting/scenarios-in-dynamic-staking#additional-information)

**Additional Information:**

#### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/dynamic-pool-accounting/scenarios-in-dynamic-staking#profit-distribution)

**Profit Distribution:**

*   **Positive Returns:** Distributed proportionally to users' stakes in sub-pools.
    
*   **Negative Returns:** Recorded as drawdowns and covered by future profits before distribution.
    
*   **Drawdown Management:** Ensures users' stakes are protected by balancing profits and losses within sub-pools.
    

#### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/dynamic-pool-accounting/scenarios-in-dynamic-staking#main-contract-and-sub-pools)

**Main Contract and Sub-Pools:**

*   **Main Contract:** Manages overall staking and coordinates with sub-pools for profit and loss distribution.
    
*   **Sub-Pools:** Handle individual stakes and cycle-specific accounting, ensuring fair distribution based on performance.
    

[PreviousDynamic Pool Accounting](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/dynamic-pool-accounting)
[NextWhat is an Accounting Window](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/what-is-an-accounting-window)

# What is an Accounting Window | STAKING MANUAL | BETFIN DOCS

_**The accounting window is a period of time that occurs once per cycle when staking revenues are counted and distributed among staking owners on the chain.**_

*   Accounting window duration may vary according to staking type and amount of staking users on the platform.
    
    *   Conservative and dynamic staking has its own accounting window as those are independent contracts.
        
    *   The accounting window for conservative staking is described in [Conservative Pool Accounting](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/conservative-pool-accounting)
        
    *   The accounting window for dynamic staking is described in [Dynamic Pool Accounting](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/dynamic-pool-accounting)
        
    
*   During the accounting window, some important restrictions affect all Betfin active members, not just those in staking.
    
    *   These restrictions may vary according to the accounting window of conservative or dynamic staking.
        
    *   See the table below that splits the effects of each action based on conservative or dynamic staking accounting window.
        
    

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/what-is-an-accounting-window#see)

SEE [Accounting Window & Terms](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-terms/accounting-window-and-terms)

# Affiliate intro | AFFILIATE MANUAL | BETFIN DOCS

Betfin affiliate intro video

Since Betfin has no central owner, recommendations are the sole way to grow the project. To support this, developers allocated 49% of all BET tokens to an affiliate program designed to boost token growth and encourage users to invite new partners.

The key idea: no one can join Betfin without an invitation from an active user. To invite someone, you must first become a client and stake BET tokens worth at least 40,000 BET. From there, you have two invitation options:

1\. Generate a non-transferrable Permit NFT token for anyone’s address.

2\. Create a unique presentation link that lets your invitees generate their own Permit NFT.

Your direct commission for each affiliate is 7% of the staked value and 0.5% of all bets.

But there’s more! After staking at least 80,000 BET and inviting users with a combined stake of 160,000 BET or more, you unlock the infinite matching binary bonus.

Binary matching is a compensation model where downline members are assigned to either a left or right team, earning you 8% of the volume from the weaker team each day. This volume includes all staking and 1% of all bets, extending from the first to infinite levels in your binary tree. Volume from the stronger leg rolls over to the next day. The only cap is a daily claim limit of 12,000,000 BET or 10% of your stake.

Best of all? It’s completely anonymous and secured by Web3!

Visit our academy ([https://betfin.network/academy](https://betfin.network/academy/advanced/)
) to learn how to expand your team’s performance and gain substantial profits daily!

[NextBetfin Pass NFT](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-explanation/betfin-pass-nft)

Last updated 11 months ago

# Staking revenue model | STAKING MANUAL | BETFIN DOCS

*   This assignment is defined by the game logic that is described in [Conservative vs Dynamic Games](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-terms/conservative-vs-dynamic-games)
    

Conservative staking revenue model

Dynamic staking revenue model

All shared games are subject to a winning fee that inflows to the conservative staking after the end of each round.

*   Check the logic in [Conservative Staking Manual](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-user-manual/conservative-staking-manual)
    
*   Check the following list of all games and their winning fee inflow to conservative staking
    

Shared game

Win fee

Partner reward

Staking reward

[Predict Game](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/predict-game)

**3,6%**

**Paid from winning fee**

**Win fee - partner reward**

[Lucky Round (LURO)](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/lucky-round-luro)

**3,6%**

**Paid from winning fee**

**Win fee - partner reward**

[Events](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/events)

**3,6%**

# Staking FAQ | STAKING MANUAL | BETFIN DOCS

Can I withdraw from the staking earlier than the predefined period?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/staking-faq#can-i-withdraw-from-the-staking-earlier-than-the-predefined-period)

No, staking runs for a defined period and there is no way to cancel such a transaction or withdraw until the staking finishes.

Consider your needs for liquidity before you stake!

What if I lost access to my wallet after I locked coins into staking?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/staking-faq#what-if-i-lost-access-to-my-wallet-after-i-locked-coins-into-staking)

If you are unable to recover your wallet access the token balance and all stakings are lost.

How can I verify that staking programs are legit?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/staking-faq#how-can-i-verify-that-staking-programs-are-legit)

Betfin contracts are audited by world respected auditor - read

All transactions such as bets or stakings are transparently visible on the blockchain.

Each betting round generates a certain profit for staking. You can track all profits and connect them to real existing bets. Check out the stats on the staking page.

Is it possible to restake my staking revenues and get compound interest?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/staking-faq#is-it-possible-to-restake-my-staking-revenues-and-get-compound-interest)

Yes, however, you need to restake your tokens manually, we have no control of your wallet and therefore you have to claim your revenues and restake it.

Where can I check the staking revenue?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/staking-faq#where-can-i-check-the-staking-revenue)

Navigate to [https://betfin.io/statistics](https://betfin.io/statistics)
 where you can find all statistics such as revenues of each cycle of both conservative and dynamic staking. Number of stakers, staked amounts and other data.

To find out more visit

[PreviousWhat is an Accounting Window](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/what-is-an-accounting-window)

# Legal Aspects of Affiliate Promotion | AFFILIATE MANUAL | BETFIN DOCS

Betfin operates as a web3 application without a central operator, and it functions as a self-executing contract. **This means there’s no direct relationship between users and a governing entity, suggesting no central party subject to regulation or compliance.**

HOWEVER...

To ensure compliance, consult your legal advisor on the best methods for promoting the Betfin platform and its partner pages.

**This is a basic framework for addressing the legal aspects of Betfin.** Below are potential questions you may wish to discuss with your legal advisor:

How to legally promote Betfin **games in your country**?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/legal-aspects-of-affiliate-promotion#how-to-legally-promote-betfin-games-in-your-country)

Consider lotto games and shared games as two separated kinds of products as those are on different principle.

How legally promote Betfin **staking in your country**?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/legal-aspects-of-affiliate-promotion#how-legally-promote-betfin-staking-in-your-country)

Consider dynamic staking and conservative staking as two separated products as those are on different principle.

How to legally participate on Betfin **affiliate in your country**?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/legal-aspects-of-affiliate-promotion#how-to-legally-participate-on-betfin-affiliate-in-your-country)

Betfin affiliate participation may bring tax and other related consequences.

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/legal-aspects-of-affiliate-promotion#options-for-adjusting-your-affiliate-strategy)

Options for Adjusting Your Affiliate Strategy


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**If your advisor finds certain aspects of your Betfin affiliate strategy legally challenging, consider revising (or, if necessary, halting) your strategy.** Here are some options to help you promote Betfin while staying within the legal framework of your jurisdiction:

1\. Feature Blocking for Compliance

*   Betfin offers the option to create a partner setup that allows specific features to be blocked on your website.
    
*   For instance, if lotto games are restricted in your country, you can design a partner page that blocks access to lotto games for users based on their IP addresses. Learn more in [Partner Contract Explained](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/for-partners/about-partner-contract/partner-contract-explained)
    .
    

2\. Shift Marketing Activities to Permissive Regions

*   If promoting Betfin within your country proves unfeasible, consider conducting your marketing activities in regions where regulations are less restrictive, allowing you to operate more freely.
    

These strategies can help you tailor your approach to align with local regulations and continue building your affiliate network responsibly.

[PreviousBuild the Team & Community](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/how-to-join-afiiliate/build-the-team-and-community)
[NextAffiliate Terms](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-terms)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Betfin Pass NFT | AFFILIATE MANUAL | BETFIN DOCS

![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F621157485-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FuG2FOxQN4xW8cuFDITeM%252Fuploads%252Fb2waufbW1bh9OeIjvQLE%252FScreenshot%25202024-03-10%2520at%252020.08.41.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D65af2ee7-7525-4867-8a8b-68cedb9b51e6&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=70a2445f&sv=2)

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-explanation/betfin-pass-nft#what-is-it)

What is it:

*   Think of the Betfin Pass Token as a unique access ticket to the Betfin platform.
    
*   The Betfin Pass (**also known as the Betfin Permit Token**) is a special type of digital token called an ERC-721, commonly referred to as an NFT (Non-Fungible Token).
    
*   Unlike regular cryptocurrencies, each NFT is unique and cannot be exchanged one-to-one with other tokens.
    
*   _Find the technical details about the Betfin pass in_ [Pass Contract](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/pass-contract)
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-explanation/betfin-pass-nft#terms)

Terms

*   The Betfin Pass is non-transferable, so any invited wallet remains a permanent member of Betfin!
    
*   Each wallet can hold only one Betfin Pass, meaning it’s not possible to invite already-invited members:
    
    *   Each Pass in a member’s wallet is linked to the inviter’s wallet.
        
    *   No one can transfer their position in the affiliate structure.
        
    *   Your members will remain in your structure for a lifetime.
        
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-explanation/betfin-pass-nft#why-it-exists)

Why it exists?

*   The Betfin Pass exists to identify Betfin members on the blockchain - only holders can access Betfin contracts, such as staking, betting, or inviting new members.
    
*   It provides the simplest way for an affiliate system to operate on the blockchain.
    

[PreviousAffiliate intro](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual)
[NextMint your pass](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-explanation/betfin-pass-nft/mint-your-pass)

# Binary Matching Example | AFFILIATE MANUAL | BETFIN DOCS

1.  **Example Structure:**
    

*   You invited user A & user B
    
*   User A invited user C and user D
    
*   User B invited user E
    

1.  **Example Volumes:**
    

*   In Cycle 1 (first day), users have the following volumes, which may result from staking or 1% of bets:
    
    *   User A has a volume of 100,000 BET
        
    *   User B has a volume of 10,000 BET
        
    *   User C has a volume of 10,000 BET
        
    *   User D has a volume of 50,000 BET
        
    *   User E has a volume of 90,000 BET
        
    

1.  **Unmatched Volume Calculation for Cycle 1:**
    

*   Your unmatched volume for this cycle is:
    
    *   Left side volume = 160,000 BET (A + C + D)
        
    *   Right side volume = 100,000 BET (B + E)
        
    

1.  **Counting of Matching for Cycle 1:**
    

*   Assuming you qualify for the matching bonus and your claim will be less than 10% of your staking amount, there’s no claim limit in this case.
    
    *   Total Volume: 260,000 BET
        
    *   Left Side Volume: 160,000 BET
        
    *   Right Side Volume: 100,000 BET
        
    
*   At the end of the day (00:00), the system takes the weaker leg - here, the right leg with 100,000 BET volume.
    
    *   Matching Bonus Calculation: 8% of the weaker leg’s volume = 8,000 BET.
        
    *   This 8,000 BET is added to your claim balance.
        
    *   The 100,000 BET matched volume is recorded.
        
    
*   Unmatched Volume for the Next Cycle:
    
    *   The remaining 60,000 BET on the left side carries over to the next cycle as unmatched volume.
        
    

![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F621157485-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FuG2FOxQN4xW8cuFDITeM%252Fuploads%252FSQ5kLhnjZxZu5bU7soV1%252F12.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df88d14ff-8c9d-4dbb-b4d1-dd61164eaa32&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=52c6de69&sv=2)

Cycle 1

1.  **Matching for the Cycle 2**
    

*   In the second cycle, there was only one change:
    
    *   A new user, F, was affiliated by user B and generated a volume of 100,000 BET.
        
    
*   The matching situation:
    
    *   Unmatched volume on the left side from the previous cycle is 60,000 BET.
        
    *   New unmatched volume on the right side is 100,000 BET from user F.
        
    
*   Matching Calculation:
    
    *   The system matches 60,000 BET from the weaker leg (left side).
        
    *   The matching bonus is 8% of 60,000 BET, resulting in a payout of 4,800 BET to your claim balance.
        
    *   The remaining unmatched volume of 40,000 BET stays on the right leg for the next cycle.
        
    

![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F621157485-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FuG2FOxQN4xW8cuFDITeM%252Fuploads%252F7e4mgOjX5JCqb4OT7oyb%252F13.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D81b9d6dc-0e9a-4de9-90f3-26c358d8d043&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=220d6735&sv=2)

Second cycle

**This principle can be applied across unlimited levels, users, and cycles, with the only restriction being the daily claim limit.**

# Affiliate FAQ | AFFILIATE MANUAL | BETFIN DOCS

Is it possible to use Betfin services without being affiliated?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-explanation/affiliate-faq#is-it-possible-to-use-betfin-services-without-being-affiliated)

No, Betfin services are available only for affiliated member.

That protects those who invest their time and energy to share Betfin vision to get affiliate rewards.

How can I recommend someone to Betfin?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-explanation/affiliate-faq#how-can-i-recommend-someone-to-betfin)

You have two options how to do it:

1.  You ask your friend for a wallet and you generate them a Betfin Permit token that connects their wallet under yours.
    
2.  You can send them a unique link that allows them to generate Betfin Permit token to their address.
    

Remember that issuance of permit token requires blockchain fee.

What is Betfin Permit Token (pass) and why it exists?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-explanation/affiliate-faq#what-is-betfin-permit-token-pass-and-why-it-exists)

Betfin Permit token (pass) is NFT (ERC 721) that works as non-transferable entrance ticket. This NFT assures you access to Betfin services for ever.

Find out more in

What are the affiliate commissions in Betfin?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-explanation/affiliate-faq#what-are-the-affiliate-commissions-in-betfin)

Direct affiliate is 7 % .

Depth affiliate is 8 % from the weaker leg in binary tree.

Maximum daily revenue is 12000 USD in BET token.

How are the affiliate commissions covered while Betfin is decentralized?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-explanation/affiliate-faq#how-are-the-affiliate-commissions-covered-while-betfin-is-decentralized)

In unique Betfin tokenomics there is a reserve of 49% of all tokens that are locked in affiliate fund smart contract making them only available to unlock by affiliate commissions.

Is it allowed to create multiple accounts?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-explanation/affiliate-faq#is-it-allowed-to-create-multiple-accounts)

Yes, you can create as many accounts as you wish.

Can affiliate conditions be changed[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-explanation/affiliate-faq#can-affiliate-conditions-be-changed)

No, affiliate conditions are valid forever unless there are tokens in affiliate reserve system which will be for a long time.

Is it possible to change the sponsor?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-explanation/affiliate-faq#is-it-possible-to-change-the-sponsor)

Unfortunately, it is not possible to change it but if you want to work with someone else you can ask your new sponsor to send you Betfin Permit token and create a new account.

What is the sorting logic in Betfin binary tree?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-explanation/affiliate-faq#what-is-the-sorting-logic-in-betfin-binary-tree)

Sorting is from up to down from left to right.

Users are always automatically filled to the first available position if you dont specify otherwise.

Can I choose the exact position of my affiliate in the Binary scheme?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-explanation/affiliate-faq#can-i-choose-the-exact-position-of-my-affiliate-in-the-binary-scheme)

Yes, this great feature is available. You can choose an end user or even a networker with existing structure. Once you specify the user which should be the binary upline of your new downline then the default sorting is applied.

What should I do If my affiliate falls into the wrong position in the binary scheme?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-explanation/affiliate-faq#what-should-i-do-if-my-affiliate-falls-into-the-wrong-position-in-the-binary-scheme)

Only possible thing is to register him for a new wallet.

Position can not be changed.

Are there some restrictions on how to promote Betfin?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-explanation/affiliate-faq#are-there-some-restrictions-on-how-to-promote-betfin)

It is your own interest to promote Betin in a peaceful and respectful way to others on the internet. Please do not use spam or incorrect information as your affiliates will probably chose different sponsor and you lose your opportunity to earn from them.

Is it possible to move affiliate account from one leg to another?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-explanation/affiliate-faq#is-it-possible-to-move-affiliate-account-from-one-leg-to-another)

No, this is not possible. Once someone is in Betfin structure their position cannot be changed.

I sent the academy (invitation) link to someone but still cannot see them in my structure (binary tree)?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-explanation/affiliate-faq#i-sent-the-academy-invitation-link-to-someone-but-still-cannot-see-them-in-my-structure-binary-tree)

After receiving the invitation the user needs to follow the instructions and mint their own pass in third step. Only then they will become members of Betfin and only then you will be able to see them in your structure and binary tree. Is it possible that some members have been invited by someone else long before you invited them and therefore they will be in someone else's structure. This cannot be changed. Each member can see who is their inviter in the member profile in the top right corner. You can also check the registration date there. Once again, the inviter or position cannot be changer. However, you can always open another account.

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-explanation/affiliate-faq#undefined)

# Direct Affiliate Bonus | AFFILIATE MANUAL | BETFIN DOCS

![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F621157485-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FuG2FOxQN4xW8cuFDITeM%252Fuploads%252Fb2waufbW1bh9OeIjvQLE%252FScreenshot%25202024-03-10%2520at%252020.08.41.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D65af2ee7-7525-4867-8a8b-68cedb9b51e6&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=70a2445f&sv=2)

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-explanation/direct-affiliate-bonus#explanation-of-direct-affiliate)

Explanation of Direct Affiliate


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   All members that [Start with Affiliate](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/how-to-join-afiiliate/start-with-affiliate#become-a-member-to-be-eligible-for-an-affiliate)
     will earn rewards for each affiliated stake or bet with no limitations or risk of being blocked.
    
*   The renumeration from direct affiliate is 7% of stakes and 0,5% of all bets.
    
*   Direct affiliate bonuses are paid to the claim balance on the affiliate page.
    
*   **Check** [Affiliate Terms](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-terms)
     **for full terms & conditions.**
    

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-explanation/direct-affiliate-bonus#technical-solution-of-direct-affiliate)

Technical Solution of Direct Affiliate


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Affiliate structure is defined by [Betfin Pass NFT](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-explanation/betfin-pass-nft)
     providing blockchain protection to ensure that each member’s structure remains unchanged.
    
*   The direct bonus is funded by which represents 49% of all tokens in the BET emission.
    
*   The direct affiliate program is governed by [Affiliate Contract](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/affiliate-contract)
     with claims executed through the [Affiliate Fund](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/affiliate-contract/affiliate-fund)
    .
    
*   The conditions for direct affiliate participation are outlined in [Affiliate Terms](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-terms)
    .
    

_The primary goal of the direct affiliate program is to provide users with financial satisfaction, enabling them to develop a robust affiliate strategy and establish Betfin affiliation as a primary income source._
