# Binary Tree & Matching Bonus | AFFILIATE MANUAL | BETFIN DOCS

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-explanation/binary-tree-and-matching-bonus#why-binary-tree)

Why Binary Tree?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   It is the most effective way to reward members for building the affiliate network.
    
*   The binary structure is easy for newcomers to replicate and highly scalable for experienced professionals.
    

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-explanation/binary-tree-and-matching-bonus#the-logic-of-the-binary-tree)

The Logic of the Binary Tree


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   The binary tree is a structure where each member has only two positions in their first line:
    
    *   The first two users you (or any of your binary partners) invite form your LEFT and RIGHT legs.
        
    *   Each new member is placed in the binary tree in a position defined by their direct inviter.
        
        *   In this structure, every member of your linear tree becomes part of your binary tree. However, not every member in your binary tree needs to be in your direct line.
            
        
    *   This means your binary tree can grow even without your active participation—an essential motivator in this system. To activate the matching bonus, you need to invite at least two users, and those two can inspire others to duplicate and expand the structure.
        
    
*   Refer to the image below to see how a linear tree translates into a binary tree.
    
    *   Note that members A-M joined in alphabetical order.
        
    *   Consider that [Matching Bonus Terms](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-terms/matching-bonus-terms#terms-of-affiliate-members-default-sorting-in-binary-tree)
         were applied.
        
    

![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F621157485-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FuG2FOxQN4xW8cuFDITeM%252Fuploads%252FSHgagH9qVGrNH1T60fpo%252FScreenshot%25202024-04-28%2520at%252011.12.45.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Deba50dba-7db5-4b18-8746-a70a9763e481&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5b0f0acc&sv=2)

The logic of linear tree to binary tree transcription according to default sorting logic

*   The binary tree and linear tree are always displayed on your affiliate page, where you can view them as either a table or a genealogy tree.
    
*   We recommend using the binary tree view when building your structure, as the linear tree view is primarily helpful for identifying who is actively inviting new members and who is not.
    

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-explanation/binary-tree-and-matching-bonus#the-matching-bonus-calculation)

The Matching Bonus Calculation


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Matching occurs once per cycle, where each cycle lasts 24 hours.
    
*   During matching, the volume of the WEAK leg is DEDUCTED from the STRONG leg, and an 8% matching bonus is paid based on the volume of the weaker leg:
    
    *   Matching bonus is 8% from the weak leg.
        
    *   Volume includes 100% of all stakes and 1% of all bets within your binary tree.
        
    *   Any remaining volume on the stronger leg carries over to future cycles with no time limit, meaning any volume you generate on your weaker leg will always yield an 8% reward.
        
    
*   The depth of users and who invited them is irrelevant; only the total volume of the left and right sides matters. Simple, right!
    
*   The matching bonus is added to your matching bonus claim balance in the affiliate section.
    

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-explanation/binary-tree-and-matching-bonus#matching-bonus-claim-and-limits)

Matching Bonus Claim and Limits


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   The maximum possible claim is 10% of your total staking amount or 12,000,000 BET based on the combined value of your conservative and dynamic staking.
    
*   There is no time limit on how long the claim balance can wait for you to claim it.
    
*   The maximum claim does not accumulate,
    
    *   so you cannot claim 100% of your staking value after 10 days of waiting;
        
    *   each day’s claim is calculated independently.
        
    *   We are considering an automated claim feature for members with over 100 million BET in staking.
        
    

[PreviousDirect Affiliate Bonus](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-explanation/direct-affiliate-bonus)
[NextBinary Matching Example](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-explanation/binary-tree-and-matching-bonus/binary-matching-example)

# Mint your pass | AFFILIATE MANUAL | BETFIN DOCS

**It is not possible to join Betfin without an invitation (without a permit token). You have to be invited by someone. There are 2 options**

**Being invited directly**

If you know anyone who is already an active Betfin member you can ask him to mint the Betfin permit token to your wallet.

*   Having a permit token in your wallet means you are invited and can join all Betfin functionalities.
    
*   The gas fee for the invitation is paid by the inviter.
    

**Receiving an invitation link**:

The invitation link will redirect you to the Betfin homepage. Here you can mint your token by yourself.

*   Simply click the button "mint your access token" and execute the transaction.
    
*   Keep in mind that you will have to pay the gas fee in MATIC for minting a permit token.
    

*   If you were already invited and can not get in then simply log in to the invited wallet and connect it to the Betfin.
    
*   You can not transfer this permit token away out of your wallet as any of your invitees won't be able to do so.
    
*   To find out more about the Betfin Permit token visit [Betfin Pass NFT](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-explanation/betfin-pass-nft)
    

[PreviousBetfin Pass NFT](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-explanation/betfin-pass-nft)
[NextDirect Affiliate Bonus](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-explanation/direct-affiliate-bonus)

# Position Strategy in the Binary Tree | AFFILIATE MANUAL | BETFIN DOCS

One great feature in Betfin’s decentralized affiliate program is that you can choose each affiliated member’s position before sending their invitation. Once a downline’s position is set after invitation, it cannot be changed.

**You have control over the placement of each member you invite**

*   There are multiple options for positioning new members; let’s go over each invitation type.
    
*   For a better understanding, we recommend reading [Binary Tree & Matching Bonus](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-explanation/binary-tree-and-matching-bonus)
     first.
    

Default position

Choose position for access generation

Choose position for invitation link

*   All users are positioned in a top-down, left-to-right order.
    
*   The system disregards any matched or unmatched volume for each member.
    
*   If you don’t specify the position of an invited member, they will automatically be placed in the first available spot in the binary tree according to this order.
    
*   As stated in [Matching Bonus Terms](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-terms/matching-bonus-terms#terms-of-affiliate-members-default-sorting-in-binary-tree)
    

**You can select the position of your invited user while generating the invitation.**

*   The new member will be placed under the specified parent user when the invitation is created.
    
    *   The parent user must already be in the system.
        
    *   The parent user should be within your network; otherwise, you won’t receive a matching bonus.
        
    
*   To choose your parent, navigate to your binary tree and select a strategic position (as shown below).
    
    ![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F621157485-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FuG2FOxQN4xW8cuFDITeM%252Fuploads%252Fu6NTyEGT6TQ5FavQLjNE%252FScreenshot%25202024-04-27%2520at%252019.38.59.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D859c3df7-3f81-4c83-96aa-be64959cb29a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b2a01259&sv=2)
    
    **Imagine you need to sign up a new user under the left leg user ending in 0x…fe8, based on the information that the right leg will be strong enough independently. This positioning allows you to build a balanced structure, optimizing for matching bonuses by reinforcing the weaker leg.**
    

![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F621157485-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FuG2FOxQN4xW8cuFDITeM%252Fuploads%252FkyRl580MNx1VyVwyuS9D%252FScreenshot%25202024-04-27%2520at%252019.40.52.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da91081e6-64ce-43d8-8c67-23cdcd236aaf&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ca1475ba&sv=2)

**Simply paste the 0x…fe8 address as the parent address, and your next downline will be positioned under this user in both your binary tree and the 0x…fe8 downline’s binary tree.**

*   If you choose a parent who already has a structure, the new member will be sorted according to [Default position](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/how-to-join-afiiliate/earn-matching-bonus/position-strategy-in-the-binary-tree#default-position)
     sorting system.
    
*   You will always receive the direct bonus, even if the user’s parent is different from you.
    

You can choose an exact position in the binary tree for all users invited through your link.

*   To set the position of new members minting access through the invitation link, use the same principles outlined in [Position Strategy in the Binary Tree](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/how-to-join-afiiliate/earn-matching-bonus/position-strategy-in-the-binary-tree#choose-position-for-direct-invitation)
    
*   However, invitation via link offers an extra feature - open any of your downline’s profile and copy their specific invitation link to make them the parent of any new invitees joining through this link. See the example below for guidance.
    

![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F621157485-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FuG2FOxQN4xW8cuFDITeM%252Fuploads%252Fu6NTyEGT6TQ5FavQLjNE%252FScreenshot%25202024-04-27%2520at%252019.38.59.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D859c3df7-3f81-4c83-96aa-be64959cb29a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b2a01259&sv=2)

**Imagine you need to invite a new user under the left leg user ending in 0x…fe8, knowing that the right leg will grow strong on its own. This strategy reinforces the weaker leg, helping balance your binary tree and optimizing matching bonuses.**

![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F621157485-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FuG2FOxQN4xW8cuFDITeM%252Fuploads%252FNmCd46uDjU31iz12zlz1%252FScreenshot%25202024-04-27%2520at%252019.53.39.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D62351c1b-24d7-42bf-97c0-23a4784a9976&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=12c0917d&sv=2)

**Open the 0x…fe8 user profile and simply copy the invitation link. This link will allow the new user to join as your direct affiliate, with 0x…fe8 set as their parent user.**

*   You will always be the direct inviter for users who join through the link with an exact binary position.
    
*   Keep in mind that any link you create cannot be revoked.
    
    *   Even if someone familiar with your structure generates an invitation link themselves, it poses no risk to you or your affiliate strategy.
        
    
*   If you set a parent with an existing structure, new members joining through the link will be positioned according to [Default position](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/how-to-join-afiiliate/earn-matching-bonus/position-strategy-in-the-binary-tree#default-position)
     sorting system.
    

How to generate invitation under certain position in the binary tree?

1\. Open the profile of the user you want to set as the parent.

2\. Copy their specific invitation link, which ensures that any new member joining through this link will be placed under that parent user in your binary tree.

3\. Share the link with your invitee, and they’ll join with the exact position you’ve chosen.

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/how-to-join-afiiliate/earn-matching-bonus/position-strategy-in-the-binary-tree#consider-the-client-or-affiliate-potential-of-your-downlines)

Consider the client or affiliate potential of your downlines.


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Your goal is to balance your left and right legs to maximize daily earnings.
    
*   Think about long-term potential - how much could they stake, bet, or contribute as affiliates to your team?
    
*   While you may not know the exact capabilities of your downlines, the numbers speak clearly - monitor the volume in your structure and focus on strengthening the weaker leg to maintain balance and optimize rewards.
    

![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F621157485-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FuG2FOxQN4xW8cuFDITeM%252Fuploads%252FOeCTDyvoUCJq6vOPohlP%252FScreenshot%25202024-04-27%2520at%252020.13.26.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2c36bf27-6571-4b44-8a0e-14d8eaedbeb4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e792cd23&sv=2)

**Imagine you notice that your right leg is consistently performing better in the long run. You can see this through the total volume generated by each of your downlines displayed in your binary tree structure. To balance this, you decide to support your left leg by inviting potential new affiliates. This approach increases the chance that they’ll generate volume and bring in additional affiliates, thereby unlocking the volume in your right leg for matching bonuses.**

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/how-to-join-afiiliate/earn-matching-bonus/position-strategy-in-the-binary-tree#motivate-your-affiliates-by-placing-new-members-in-a-single-line-within-one-leg)

Motivate your affiliates by placing new members in a single line within one leg.


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   The strongest motivation for a new user is seeing one of their legs grow passively.
    
*   By building one leg for your members, they only need to focus on growing the second leg themselves.
    
*   The best strategy is to sort all your direct members one below another within either your left or right leg, helping them establish a solid foundation for future growth.
    

[PreviousEarn Matching Bonus](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/how-to-join-afiiliate/earn-matching-bonus)
[NextBuild the Team & Community](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/how-to-join-afiiliate/build-the-team-and-community)

# Build the Team & Community | AFFILIATE MANUAL | BETFIN DOCS

BetFin is a purely technological platform, and its success relies on active community builders. At the same time, BetFin has the potential to positively impact lives, and its affiliate program is designed to generously reward community leaders.

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/how-to-join-afiiliate/build-the-team-and-community#what-is-community-and-its-purpose)

What is Community and its Purpose?

*   A community is a group of people who share the same values, vision, and interests.
    
*   Communities can be online or offline and range from a few individuals to millions.
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/how-to-join-afiiliate/build-the-team-and-community#how-to-start-building-a-community)

How to Start Building a Community?

• Generate Income: Start by earning through staking and affiliate activities, allowing you to move away from tasks you don’t enjoy.

• Connect with Others: Engage with the first people interested in Betfin, whether it’s your sponsor or downlines. (A chat feature will be added soon on betfin.io)

• Develop a Community-Building Strategy: Focus on the key elements outlined in the table below to grow and sustain your community.

This approach will help you build a thriving community and capitalize on the rewards BetFin offers to active leaders!

Generate leads

Explain Betfin

Onboarding

Duplication

Generating leads is the first, though not the only, essential step to building your team and community. The number and quality of leads directly influence the growth rate of your team.

#### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/how-to-join-afiiliate/build-the-team-and-community#how-to-develop-a-lead-generation-strategy)

How to Develop a Lead Generation Strategy

To craft a successful lead generation strategy, review your available resources, experience, and environment. If you’re uncertain, reach out to us for support. Here are a few tips to kickstart your lead generation campaign based on your specific environment:

Lead generation offline

Lead generation online - passive growth

Although Betfin is an online platform, incorporating offline elements can elevate your lead generation campaign significantly. Here are some simple tips for generating leads offline:

1.  Reach Out to Close Contacts: Start with your friends and family—let them know you’ve found something they won’t want to miss!
    
2.  Offer a Fun Introduction: Send them a few of your BET tokens to enjoy some Betfin games together. We suggest trying a shared game to highlight the social aspect.
    
3.  Showcase Staking Results: Share your staking outcomes and suggest they start by staking a few tokens (an affordable amount for them, though 120,000BET is recommended to pre-open their binary tree).
    
4.  Reconnect After Initial Payouts: Once you receive some payouts, follow up to discuss how they can bring in leads to earn affiliate bonuses. This is where your lead generation structure begins to grow.
    
5.  Highlight Growth Potential: Show your direct affiliates they already have unmatched volume in their binary structure—waiting to be matched. This can motivate them to bring in two direct members, transforming your effort into a six-member team, creating a steady income for you.
    

_Then, you can take your offline lead generation to a professional level by organizing a presentation or hosting an offline event for the community. For support with this, feel free to contact us anytime at magnum@betfin.io._

*   **We recommend bringing your offline contacts to an online presentation or an offline event to let them experience the Betfin community.**
    
*   **Connect your downlines to Betfin’s social media channels so they can stay informed on project updates and see how it’s growing.**
    

Online lead generation focuses on drawing downlines to reach out to you or delivering leads directly to you rather than pursuing them yourself. Here are some strategies for effective and engaging online lead generation:

1.  **Utilise Social Media Powerfully** - Let's expect you utilised the maximum of your friends and family as explained in [Lead generation offline](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/how-to-join-afiiliate/build-the-team-and-community#lead-generation-offline)
     - Use social media to let your followers know you’ve started an exciting new business - Focus on attracting interest so people come to you, rather than pursuing new partners directly. You can do this collaboratively with some of your team members
    
2.  **Don't spam the project;** instead, create an air of exclusivity - without a BetFin Pass, no one can join!
    
3.  **Attract with Lifestyle and Success Online** - Share glimpses of your success, such as winnings, staking rewards, and community growth. - Leverage BetFin’s blockchain transparency to show real results, sparking curiosity and interest.
    
4.  **Consider Automation**
    

\-Automate lead generation through your own landing pages, email retargeting campaigns, etc.

\-Use BetFin-provided videos and materials to enhance engagement.

\-Create a website to introduce BetFin to potential partners, guiding them to explore the vision and join.

**Once your lead generation campaign is set up, it’s time to start earning!**

• **Set a Target Number of Leads:** Establish a clear goal for leads to measure your campaign’s success.

• **Calculate Your Conversion Rate:** Track how many leads turn into active partners or clients.

• **Identify and Address Weak Points:** Analyze any areas of low conversion to make adjustments for better results.

• **Refine and Relaunch:** Improve your campaign based on insights and launch the next round for ongoing growth.

**You don’t need expert knowledge of Betfin to promote it.** BetFin’s documentation and videos are designed to explain everything on your behalf. Your mission is to let your downlines know that you recommend and trust the project. Here are some tips:

*   **Avoid over-explaining, as Betfin provides high-quality resources for understanding the platform:**
    
    *   Use Betfin’s official videos.
        
    *   Refer to Betfin documentation.
        
    *   Invite them to Betfin community webinars.
        
    *   Encourage attendance at Betfin community offline events.
        
    
*   **Best Approach for Understanding and Conviction**
    
    *   The simplest way to help your downlines understand and feel confident is to let them try it firsthand.
        
    *   Offer them some BET tokens and MATIC for free, play a game together, or let them stake a few tokens for fun.
        
    *   This hands-on experience can naturally encourage them to stake a bit more.
        
    
*   **Respect Downline Preferences**
    
    *   For those hesitant about investing-based earnings, avoid pressuring them to play with real money.
        
    *   For those interested primarily in gambling, focus on the gaming aspect, introducing earnings only if they express interest.
        
    

The hardest part of community growth is onboarding—turning a potential member into an active one.

1.  Be prepared to direct your new downline to
    
    1.  Use documentation in their native language if available (if not, it’s an opportunity for you to assist)
        
    
2.  Guide your downline to
    

Once a member is satisfied as a client, converting them into an affiliate partner becomes much easier, empowering them to duplicate your efforts. Duplication is a critical success factor in BetFin’s affiliate program.

#### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/how-to-join-afiiliate/build-the-team-and-community#how-to-support-duplication)

How to Support Duplication?

*   [Position Strategy in the Binary Tree](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/how-to-join-afiiliate/earn-matching-bonus/position-strategy-in-the-binary-tree#motivate-your-affiliated-members-by-loading-your-new-members-to-one-line)
    
*   Encourage Community Resources: Guide your team to utilize community webinars and events rather than creating their own until they achieve a high level of knowledge.
    
*   Regular Communication: Connect with your team across your structure regularly, ideally once a week, sharing both successes and challenges.
    
*   Transfer Goals: Once you reach your goals, pass them on to your downlines and actively help them achieve the same.
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/how-to-join-afiiliate/build-the-team-and-community#help-your-downline-members-to-grow)

Help Your Downline Members to Grow

To accelerate community growth, it’s essential that your downlines feel motivated and enjoy their progress. Leverage the power of the Betfin binary tree and inspire your downlines to expand their networks.

*   Encourage Resource Use: Instead of requiring them to know everything, guide them to the documentation for support.
    
*   Highlight Betfin Support: Show them that they can close deals using Betfin’s resources, including online presentations and events, without needing in-depth knowledge or presentation skills.
    
*   Lead by Example: Share your success stories to inspire, and teach them how to duplicate this within their own teams.
    
*   Provide Non-Financial Incentives: Offer rewards or recognition for top community leaders. This non-financial motivation will come back a hundredfold in dedication and growth.
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/how-to-join-afiiliate/build-the-team-and-community#focus-on-culture)

Focus on Culture

A key aspect of building a strong community is fostering a positive culture. Business culture includes many elements but is always rooted in strong relationships among community members. This is built on shared personal values and a commitment to a common vision.

Key Features to Empower Community Culture

1.  **Online Webinars and Presentations** \- Host, join, or organize webinars and presentations. These can focus on specific Betfin game events or serve as introductions for new members.
    
2.  **Offline Events** \- Offline events allow for personal connections with top community leaders, who often host these gatherings.
    
3.  **Team Leisure Activities -** Strengthen personal bonds by organizing non-business-focused activities with your team. - Leisure activities are an ideal way to build trust and connection.
    
4.  **Open Community Offices for Personal Meetings** \- Set up community offices for personal meetings. Share these locations on the official Betfin Telegram to connect with the central community. - Your offices could become part of the official Betfin office structure, elevating your work to a serious business level.
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/how-to-join-afiiliate/build-the-team-and-community#connect-with-other-communities)

Connect with Other Communities

*   Engage with other community leaders on social media to build connections and strengthen the community network. Collaborating with other leaders fosters a more unified and resilient community.
    
*   Find Betfin’s partnering communities on social media.

# Start with Affiliate | AFFILIATE MANUAL | BETFIN DOCS

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/how-to-join-afiiliate/start-with-affiliate#steps-to-get-started)

Steps to get started:


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Become a Member:** You need to be a member to qualify for the affiliate program.
    
*   **Stake BET Tokens:** Stake a minimum of 40,000 BET in conservative and/or dynamic staking.
    
    *   See the [Direct Affiliate Terms](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-terms/direct-affiliate-terms)
        for detailed conditions.
        
    
*   _Note that it may take a few minutes for blockchain data to load in the UI._
    
*   **Invite Members:** Once you’re set up, start inviting your first members:
    

Make direct invitation

Generate invitation link

_Direct invitation involves minting the Betfin Pass Token to someone’s address. The process is straightforward. You can choose to mint the token to one or multiple addresses, allowing you to invite your downlines in a single transaction!_

Invite a single member

Bulk invitation

Visit your affiliate page and generate the Betfin Pass to your invitee’s wallet. This action will make the invitee your downline, granting them lifetime eligibility to use BetFin contracts.

![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F621157485-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FuG2FOxQN4xW8cuFDITeM%252Fuploads%252For0dvV8XpMDhp8wHNqEX%252FScreenshot%25202024-04-27%2520at%252018.30.26.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De60cfcfa-3a5d-4331-a7fd-812e0a80235f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b4c1e2be&sv=2)

Paste invitee Polygon (MATIC) address and click generate

*   You can repeat this process unlimited times or, if you have many users to invite at once, try using [Bulk invitation](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/how-to-join-afiiliate/start-with-affiliate#bulk-invitation)
     instead
    

To execute a bulk invitation:

1.  Download the sample bulk permit mint table (the CSV format is simple: each row should include `parent,new_member` ).
    
2.  Fill in your invitees’ data.
    
3.  Upload the completed CSV file to the Betfin interface.
    
4.  Execute the bulk invitation transaction.
    

![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F621157485-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FuG2FOxQN4xW8cuFDITeM%252Fuploads%252F9TtfxTbNl39U9xrr9lwX%252FScreenshot%25202024-04-27%2520at%252018.37.16.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9c51f280-2869-44f5-b7c9-9079949bd947&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1b3d8e31&sv=2)

*   Keep in mind there is a limit of approximately 100 invitations per transaction due to the GAS limit on the Polygon blockchain
    
*   Executing these transactions may incur higher gas fees in MATIC, which you will need to cover from your own resources.
    
*   Also, ensure that the parent user is already in the system or listed earlier in the CSV file, or the transaction will fail.
    

_Generating an invitation link is simple. Just click on “Copy link” on your affiliate page once you’ve completed step 1._

![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F621157485-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FuG2FOxQN4xW8cuFDITeM%252Fuploads%252Fwvyjc5J6bxA3TKveXm5F%252FScreenshot%25202024-04-27%2520at%252018.16.10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddaf66448-7fc6-46ae-aced-ad1491d6fd9f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b98ac554&sv=2)

Click this button to copy your invitation link

*   Once you have the link, you can share it with anyone you wish to invite.
    
    *   They’ll be directed to the Betfin.io landing page, where they can mint the BetFin Pass NFT.
        
    *   Keep in mind that your partner will need to cover the MATIC gas fee to mint the access token.
        
    *   If your partner is new to crypto, we recommend [Start with Affiliate](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/how-to-join-afiiliate/start-with-affiliate#how-to-invite-someone-directly)
        and sending them a small amount of MATIC and BET tokens to help them get started.
        
    

*   Keep in mind that you cannot invite an already invited user or change your or their position..
    
*   We recommend reviewing [Position Strategy in the Binary Tree](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/how-to-join-afiiliate/earn-matching-bonus/position-strategy-in-the-binary-tree)
     to learn how to manage invitations effectively and build a long-term profitable affiliate strategy.
    

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/how-to-join-afiiliate/start-with-affiliate#claim-your-first-rewards)

**Claim Your First Rewards**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Claiming your rewards is simple - just click the “Claim” button on your affiliate page.
    
*   This button covers both the 7% commission on each direct affiliate’s stake and 0.5% on each bet.
    
*   Refer to [Direct Affiliate Terms](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-terms/direct-affiliate-terms)
     for more details.
    

![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F621157485-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FuG2FOxQN4xW8cuFDITeM%252Fuploads%252FfzF7Y1BSwusOkFh5jdcn%252FScreenshot%25202024-04-27%2520at%252018.47.07.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcd23ffcf-b2d6-45cd-9bac-ba42bdebd835&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=de7042c2&sv=2)

Don’t forget that you’ll need to pay MATIC gas fees for each claim; however, there is no time or size limit on direct affiliate claims.

# Earn Matching Bonus | AFFILIATE MANUAL | BETFIN DOCS

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/how-to-join-afiiliate/earn-matching-bonus#qualify-for-the-matching-bonus)

**Qualify for the Matching Bonus**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Stake at least 120,000 BET in the conservative and/or dynamic staking program
    
*   Invite at least two members who each stake a minimum of 120,000 BET
    

This qualification unlocks the infinite binary matching program, allowing you to earn an 8% bonus on the volume of your weaker leg.

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/how-to-join-afiiliate/earn-matching-bonus#understand-the-power-of-the-infinite-binary-tree)

**Understand the Power of the Infinite Binary Tree!**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   If you’re unsure about how the binary tree works, check out the [Affiliate intro](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual)
     video for a quick overview, or dive deeper to learn more about maximizing its potential.
    
*   Once you understand this powerful business instrument, you’re halfway to success.
    

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/how-to-join-afiiliate/earn-matching-bonus#create-a-strategy-and-duplicate)

**Create a Strategy and Duplicate**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Once you duplicate your affiliate strategy across both legs, you’re well on your way.
    
*   To generate substantial income, focus on duplicating your approach and harnessing the power of the binary tree.
    
*   For more on this, check out [Build the Team & Community](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/how-to-join-afiiliate/build-the-team-and-community)
    .
    

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/how-to-join-afiiliate/earn-matching-bonus#claim-your-daily-rewards)

**Claim Your Daily Rewards**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Remember to claim your daily rewards, as the daily claim limit is the only cap on your matching bonus:
    
    *   You can claim up to 10% of your staked volume or tokens, up to a value of 12,000,000 BET.
        
    *   For further details, refer to [Matching Bonus Terms](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-terms/matching-bonus-terms)
        .
        
    

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/how-to-join-afiiliate/earn-matching-bonus#reinvest-and-multiply)

Reinvest and Multiply


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   After each claim, re-stake your rewards to maximize earnings and boost your daily claim.
    
*   Multiply your tokens by betting;
    
*   and don’t forget to sell some tokens to enjoy your profits! ⛵✈️🏖️

# Games Intro Video | GAMES MANUAL | BETFIN DOCS

Betfin games intro video

[https://firebasestorage.googleapis.com/v0/b/betfin-dev.appspot.com/o/Betfin\_Join%20the%20Game.mp4?alt=media&token=8fbb5ac4-5882-4340-b918-bd7d778a5f22firebasestorage.googleapis.com](https://firebasestorage.googleapis.com/v0/b/betfin-dev.appspot.com/o/Betfin_Join%20the%20Game.mp4?alt=media&token=8fbb5ac4-5882-4340-b918-bd7d778a5f22)

Betfin video content

_Betfin is a WEB3 betting technology based on fairness, decentralization and transparency. All games are 100% provably fair with a 100% autonomous immutable and irreversible decision system. All Betfin smart contracts can be split for 2 main categories: shared betting and decentralized lotto games._

_Shared betting means betting among users such as betting on events. Great example is crypto predict game. Imagine you have 5 minutes to bet if the BTC price goes up or down within the next 15 minutes. platform downloads the rate from Chainlink data feed and automatically evaluates the result. If you are right then you win the part of opposite bets. All winnings are subject to a winning fee which goes to conservative staking. On the other hand lotto games include all popular games like roulette, keno or slots. All those games work on the similar principle and that is random number generation from Chainlink. Users are being paid out of the dynamic staking pool. That makes the game provably fair and decentralized._

_Try the Betfin betting technology and enjoy the gambling solution of the future!_

# Matching Bonus Terms | AFFILIATE MANUAL | BETFIN DOCS

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-terms/matching-bonus-terms#settings-of-binary-matching-bonus)

Settings of Binary Matching Bonus


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Similar to** [Settings of Direct Affiliate](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-terms/direct-affiliate-terms#settings-of-direct-affiliate)
**, the binary matching contract includes options to adjust certain terms. The table below outlines the current settings as well as the highest and lowest possible limits that can be configured within the contract. These adjustments are controlled to maintain balance within the program while allowing flexibility for growth.**

Current matching terms

Limits of matching terms

Current settings of T&C for matching bonus is the following

Term

Settings

Explanation

Matching qualification condition N.1

Stake min 80,000 BET

Stake the value of at least 80,000 BET

Matching qualification condition N.2

Have 2 direct members

Affiliate at least 2 direct users

Matching qualification condition N.3

Min direct user stake 80,000 BET

Each affiliated user should stake at least for 80,000 BET

Cycle limit for claim

10% of staked value or 8,000,000 BET

1.  You cannot claim an amount larger than 10% of your staked value or 120k USD in any day
    
2.  Any unclaimed matching bonus has no expiration and will remain available.
    
3.  Your active staking sum determines the maximum BET you can claim each cycle.
    

**Following table shows the limited of T&C setting for binary matching.**

*   BetFin dev team set this limit with respect of possible expected price deviation of BET token
    

Term

Minimal settings

Maximal settings

Matching qualification condition N.1

1,000 BET

10,000,000 BET

Matching qualification condition N.2

2

2

Matching qualification condition N.3

1,000 BET

10,000,000 BET

Claim limit / cycle N.1

10% of staked value

10% of staked value

Claim limit / cycle N.2

500,000 BET

1,000,000,000 BET

*   To qualify for the binary matching bonus, a user must meet all three qualification conditions.
    
*   The claim limit per cycle will always be the lower of the two possible limits (10% of staked value or 120 million BET).
    
*   Unused claim limits do not accumulate across cycles.
    

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-terms/matching-bonus-terms#binary-matching-hardcoded-terms)

Binary Matching Hardcoded Terms


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**To maximize user protection, certain terms are irreversibly hardcoded into the contract. These fixed terms ensure stability and cannot be changed. The following table outlines these terms:**

Term

Hard-coded settings

Explanation

Matching commission

8% of week leg volume

8% commission on the total volume of the weaker leg in each cyclecle

Volume from stakes

100%

100% value of any staking realised in any depth of the binary tree is counted as the volume for matching purpose

Volume from bets

1%

100% of the value of any staking activity at any depth within the binary tree is counted as volume

Cycle length

24 hours

Each cycle is defined as a 24-hour period

Unmatched volume expiration

none

Unmatched volume in stronger leg has no expiration

*   If a user does not claim within a cycle, the opportunity remains open, as there is no expiration on unclaimed rewards.
    
*   However, each affiliate claim incurs a MATIC gas fee, payable with each individual claim.
    

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-terms/matching-bonus-terms#terms-of-default-member-sorting-in-binary-tree)

**T**erms of Default Member Sorting in Binary Tree


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Sorting Order:** All users are placed in the binary tree from top to bottom and left to right.
    
*   **Position Independence:** The system does not consider the volume or potential of each member in this sorting.
    
*   **Automatic Positioning:** If no specific position is chosen for an invited member, they will automatically be placed in the first available spot according to the top-down, left-right rule.
    

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-terms/matching-bonus-terms#note-on-binary-tree-logic)

Note on Binary Tree Logic


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   The binary tree logic is strictly applied for calculating the matching bonus and cannot be altered.
    
*   Matching calculations are executed off-chain due to the int256 limit, ensuring efficient processing without blockchain constraints.
    

[PreviousDirect Affiliate Terms](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-terms/direct-affiliate-terms)

# How to play roulette single-player | GAMES MANUAL | BETFIN DOCS

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/roulette/how-to-play-roulette-single-player#make-sure-you-know-the)

_**Make sure you know the**_


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   _Connect your invited address via the web3 wallet to the betfin page_
    
*   _Hold some BET tokens_
    
*   _Hold at least some MATIC balance to pay the gas fees_
    
*   _Set allowance for the platform_
    

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/roulette/how-to-play-roulette-single-player#go-to-roulette-page)

**Go to roulette Page**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [https://betfin.io/roulette](https://betfin.io/roulette)
    
*   you can also play roulette through any BetFin partner which use the same contract & liquidity.
    

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/roulette/how-to-play-roulette-single-player#place-a-bet)

**Place a Bet**:


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Each bet has its payout coefficient in case you correctly guess the random number.
    
*   You can play one bet or combine them according to your betting strategy.
    
*   Each bet has minimal and maximal size to protect platform sustainability.
    

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/roulette/how-to-play-roulette-single-player#waiting-for-result)

**Waiting for result**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Each round in the roulette generates unique random number through random number generation (RNG) algorithm which is fully transparent in Betfin
    
*   Check more about RNG here: [Random Number Generation](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/proof-of-fairness/random-number-generation)
    
    *   Generation of random number may take 5-30 seconds but sometimes it may be even more.
        
    *   Betfin has no control of this but that is what makes the game 100% fair (random & independent)
        
    

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/roulette/how-to-play-roulette-single-player#winning-payouts)

**Winning payouts**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   If users win, they are paid out from the dynamic staking pool
    
*   If users lose, their bets are added to the dynamic staking pool.
    
*   Understand the transparency here: [Lotto Round & Winners Protection](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/proof-of-fairness/lotto-round-and-winners-protection)
    

[PreviousRoulette](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/roulette)
[NextRoulette T&C](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/roulette/roulette-t-and-c)

# Predict Explanation | GAMES MANUAL | BETFIN DOCS

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/predict-game/predict-explanation#predict-rounds-and-logic)

PREDICT ROUNDS AND LOGIC


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Round is a time where you can place a bet. Usually 270 seconds.
    
    *   In the start of the round the START PRICE is downloaded (se [Chainlink & Datafeeds](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/proof-of-fairness/chainlink-and-datafeeds)
        )
        
    
*   During the round you bet if the price will be higher or lower after 3 rounds passes.
    
    *   Therefore after the round ends you wait 3 more rounds before the draw is made.
        
    
*   In the end of the 4th round the final price is compared with the start price of the 1st round and the draw is made
    

![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1825326731-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSinPZEOuPy8TM9anY3n8%252Fuploads%252Fz6TvMXBbsH7CV6RTDQkQ%252FScreenshot%25202024-02-03%2520at%252018.50.25.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D79af4ed9-07cd-48fc-a355-cf669c138daa&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cfeca1c1&sv=2)

PRedict round logic graphical explanation

*   You can see that rounds create an infinite chain of rounds.
    
    *   End price of 1st round represents the start price of the second round, etc.
        
    

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/predict-game/predict-explanation#draw-and-winnings-distribution)

Draw and winnings distribution


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Draw is made in the end of the 4th round
    
    *   All bets and bonuses that were placed are shared among winers (that bet on correct side)
        
    *   Participants who wins receive their winnings to their wallet address
        
    *   Winning fee of 3,6% is already deducted and transparently distributed into staking
        
    
*   To understand this further read the [Example](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/predict-game/predict-explanation/example)
    

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/predict-game/predict-explanation#predict-bonus-explanation)

Predict bonus explanation


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Lets ask yourself a question: _"__**Why should you risk and bet into pool first while there are no other bet that you can win**__"?_ _Well, the answer is that the earlier you bet the more you can win!_

*   Bonus pool collects 4% of all predict BETs and proportionally splits it among winners according to following parameters:
    
    *   How much they bet (amount of bet)
        
    *   On which place they bet (in descending way of counting - if there is 100 bets the first has value of 100 and last have value of 1)
        
    

![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1825326731-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSinPZEOuPy8TM9anY3n8%252Fuploads%252FD2UmTRMflRGUgbOx61hQ%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D80c1d057-d842-469a-ab98-82ab693a1ba5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=12d03004&sv=2)

Example of bonus pool distribution

*   That means that more you bet and earlier you bet the bigger share of the 4% bonus pool you receive in case you win.
    
    *   These 4% can also exceed your 3,6% winning fee as bonus is paid only to the winners.
        
    *   That motivates users to create bets and bring the liquidity in early stage of the round and that makes the round winning pool interesting.
        
    

[PreviousPredict Game](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/predict-game)
[NextExample](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/predict-game/predict-explanation/example)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Predict Game | GAMES MANUAL | BETFIN DOCS

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/predict-game#the-game)

The Game


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Our game is a conservative staking-related prediction market focusing on the BTC/USD pair. Each round lasts for 270 seconds, where participants place bets on the future price movement of BTC/USD. The rates are determined solely by the users in each round, ensuring a community-driven experience.

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/predict-game#why-you-should-try-it)

Why You Should Try It


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Aspect

Description

**Excitement and Engagement**

**Thrilling Experience:** Engage in the thrill of predicting market movements and competing with others. **Real-Time Action:** Participate in real-time markets and see the impact of your predictions as events unfold.

**Financial Incentives**

**Potential Rewards:** Earn rewards if your predictions are accurate. **Bonus Pools:** Additional incentives through bonus pools, increasing your potential earnings.

**Transparency and Security**

**Blockchain Technology:** Ensures all transactions are transparent, immutable, and secure. **Fair and Trustworthy:** No middlemen, ensuring a fair betting environment.

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/predict-game#how-to-bet)

How to Bet


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/predict-game#step-1-choose-a-game)

**Step 1: Choose a Game**

#### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/predict-game#explore-available-games)

**Explore Available Games:**

*   Each game represents a market where you can place your bets.
    
*   Use the `getGames` function to view all available games.
    
*   Example: `predict.getGames()`
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/predict-game#step-2-place-your-bet)

**Step 2: Place Your Bet**

1.  **Prepare Your Bet:**
    
    *   Decide on the amount you want to bet.
        
    *   Choose whether you believe the price will go up (long) or down (short).
        
    *   Identify the game you want to bet on.
        
    
2.  **Execute the Bet:**
    
    *   Use the `placeBet` function to place your bet.
        
    *   Provide your player address, bet amount, and game address.
        
    *   Example: `predict.placeBet(playerAddress, betAmount, gameAddress)`
        
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/predict-game#step-3-monitor-your-bet)

**Step 3: Monitor Your Bet**

1.  **Check Your Bets:**
    
    *   Use the `getPlayerBets` function to view all your bets for a specific round.
        
    *   Example: `predictGame.getPlayerBets(playerAddress, round)`
        
    
2.  **Track Bet Status:**
    
    *   Check the status and details of your bet using the `getBetInfo` function.
        
    *   Example: `predictBet.getBetInfo()`
        
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/predict-game#step-4-winning-and-payouts)

**Step 4: Winning and Payouts**

1.  **Bet Calculation:**
    
    *   Bets are calculated at the end of each round based on price movements.
        
    
2.  **Claim Rewards:**
    
    *   If your bet wins, your rewards will be automatically transferred to your wallet, including any bonus earnings.
        
    

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/predict-game#the-bonus-system)

The Bonus System


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To make the game even more exciting and rewarding, we have implemented a bonus system. Here’s how it works:

*   **Bonus Pool:** A portion of the total bet amount is allocated to a bonus pool for each round.
    
*   **Additional Earnings:** Winners not only earn their share of the main pool but also receive additional rewards from the bonus pool.
    
*   **Proportional Distribution:** The bonus is distributed proportionally based on the amount bet and the position of the bet in the round.
    

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/predict-game#contact-and-support)

Contact and Support


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you have any questions or need assistance, our support team is here to help. Reach out to us for any issues or queries regarding the Predict Betting Platform.

Happy Betting!

* * *

This guide provides a comprehensive overview of our Predict Betting Platform. For more detailed technical documentation, please refer to our official documentation or contact our support team.

[NextPredict Explanation](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/predict-game/predict-explanation)

# Lucky Round (LURO) | GAMES MANUAL | BETFIN DOCS

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/lucky-round-luro#introduction-to-lucky-round)

Introduction to Lucky Round

Lucky Round (LURO) is a live lottery game that lasts fixed period of time and is fully decentralised. The goal is to place a bet and buy a share in the current round. The more you bet, the higher your chance of winning.

![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1825326731-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSinPZEOuPy8TM9anY3n8%252Fuploads%252F7M0GNseh8TutImZFibdB%252FScreenshot%25202024-07-14%2520at%252010.19.48.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D41b474ab-d3e0-4a53-b7d7-f54e023e5168&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9478106b&sv=2)

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/lucky-round-luro#how-the-game-works)

How the Game Works

1.  **Starting the Round**: Each round of Lucky Round has fixed duration (can be 5 minutes or 1 day - see in [LURO Terms](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/lucky-round-luro/luro-terms)
    . Once the round starts, players can begin betting.
    
2.  **Betting**: During the round, players can place any amount of bet. Each bet represents a share in the round, and the more you bet, the higher your chance of winning. Each user has a unique color, representing their share and probability of winning.
    
3.  **Winner Announcement**: After Round ends, the random number is generated by CHAINLINK VRF and based on this the winner is chosen. Winner wins 95% of all bets from that round. The remaining 5% forms a bonus.
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/lucky-round-luro#betting)

Betting

#### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/lucky-round-luro#how-to-bet)

How to Bet:

1.  **Connect Wallet**: Connect your wallet to Betfin.
    
2.  **Select Timeframe**: Choose the active timeframe you want to bet in.
    
3.  **Place Bet**: Enter the amount you wish to bet and wait for confirmation through your wallet.
    

#### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/lucky-round-luro#betting-tips)

Betting Tips:

*   Bet regularly to increase your chances of winning.
    
*   Place your bets early in the round to take advantage of the bonus.
    
*   Split your bets into multiple rounds to diversify your chances.
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/lucky-round-luro#winner-announcement)

Winner Announcement

1.  **End of Round**: After the round time finishes. No further bets are accepted.
    
2.  **Random Selection**: The system randomly selects a winner from the players who bet in that round. This selection is transparent and recorded on the blockchain. The winner is announced as soon as the random number is received from Chainlink VRF.
    
3.  **Winner Notification**: The winner is notified, and 95% of all bets from that round are automatically transferred to their account. The remaining 5% is distributed as a bonus. Additionally, 3.6% of the winnings are allocated to conservative staking.
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/lucky-round-luro#bonus)

Bonus

*   **Allocation**: 5% of the total bets in a round form the bonus pool.
    
*   **Logic**: Bonus is distributed according to coeficient of size and order of bets. First bet out of 10 will have order coeficient of 10 and last will have coeficient of 1. Size coeficient matches the bet size.
    

![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1825326731-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSinPZEOuPy8TM9anY3n8%252Fuploads%252FXAYLc43N86i5MksOF3BF%252FScreenshot%25202024-07-14%2520at%252010.20.43.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8008f600-0f61-4a6e-a821-f0da15443f6c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=dcc8a56c&sv=2)

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/lucky-round-luro#security-and-transparency)

Security and Transparency

*   **Decentralization**: Lucky Round is a fully decentralized game, meaning no central authority can manipulate the results or revert bets
    
*   **Blockchain**: All bets and results are recorded on the blockchain, ensuring full transparency and security.
    
*   **Randomness**: Winners are chosen randomly - see [Random Number Generation](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/proof-of-fairness/random-number-generation)
    by chainlink VRF
    
*   **Contribution to Staking**: 3.6% of the winnings are allocated to conservative staking.
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/lucky-round-luro#support)

Support

If you have any questions or need assistance, feel free to contact our support through the Lucky Round website.

Enjoy the game and good luck!

* * *

We hope this manual helps you easily and quickly get involved in the Lucky Round game. Happy betting!

[PreviousSPLIT](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/roulette/roulette-t-and-c/split)
[NextLURO Terms](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/lucky-round-luro/luro-terms)

# Games FAQ | GAMES MANUAL | BETFIN DOCS

Can I place bets in other cryptos than just BET token?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/games-faq#can-i-place-bets-in-other-cryptos-than-just-bet-token)

It is not possible as all transactions are settled in BET tokens.

You can buy your BET tokens on Uniswap.

Can Betfin block my winnings?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/games-faq#can-betfin-block-my-winnings)

*   No, it is not possible under any circumstances.
    

Can I be banned from betting?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/games-faq#can-i-be-banned-from-betting)

No, it is not possible under any circumstances.

You can use any Betfin service as long as you have a Permit token and BET balance to play.

Is it possible to reverse or refund my bet in certain cases?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/games-faq#is-it-possible-to-reverse-or-refund-my-bet-in-certain-cases)

Unfortunately, once the bet is placed and confirmed by blockchain it is not possible to reverse in any case. There is noone that could refund you as you interact with other users and stakers through the blockchain. Therefore no refunds are available

Can anyone stop the flow of games of Betin?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/games-faq#can-anyone-stop-the-flow-of-games-of-betin)

stoppingOnce a Betfin game is deployed to the blockchain it is unstoppable. Blocking the flow of contracts would mean to stop the whole blockchain that it runs on.

Are there any limits for betting?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/games-faq#are-there-any-limits-for-betting)

Each game has individual minimal and maximal betting limits. See [GAMES TERMS](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-terms/conservative-vs-dynamic-games)
.

Where can I find the game rules?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/games-faq#where-can-i-find-the-game-rules)

Rules of each game is described in [GAMES GUIDE](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/predict-game)

Can I bet on oposite sides in case of shared betting?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/games-faq#can-i-bet-on-oposite-sides-in-case-of-shared-betting)

Yes, you have no limits just note that there is a winning fee.

What if there is an undefined round result such as tie on bitcoin predict?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/games-faq#what-if-there-is-an-undefined-round-result-such-as-tie-on-bitcoin-predict)

In that case, all the bets are reverted without any fee and affection of bonus.

[NextConservative vs Dynamic Games](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-terms/conservative-vs-dynamic-games)

# Events | GAMES MANUAL | BETFIN DOCS

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/events#overview)

Overview


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

“Events” is a thrilling prediction-based game where players place bets on the outcomes of various real-world events. From sports matches to global political milestones, participants can test their intuition and analysis in predicting outcomes. This game allows for betting on major events, like the US Elections 2024, where players can place bets on candidates such as Donald Trump or Kamala Harris.

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/events#how-the-game-works)

How the Game Works


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For purpose of this guide we will use an example of the event "US Elections 2024".

![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1825326731-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSinPZEOuPy8TM9anY3n8%252Fuploads%252Fqx2BwFzW0XjBfDqMFJ18%252FScreenshot%25202024-10-17%2520at%252007.37.47.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1b6f372b-81cd-410b-b76c-d99414b24ad9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=54e54975&sv=2)

You can find all important info on the initial screen, top to bottom:

1.  Name of the event.
    
2.  Date of the event.
    
3.  Possible outcomes you can bet on.
    
4.  Countdown showing how much time there is left to place a bet.
    
5.  Statistics - you can see other user's bets and their total volume.
    

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/events#how-to-bet)

How to bet


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Connect Wallet**: Connect your wallet to Betfin.
    
2.  **Select an Event:** Choose from a list of active events. The game will feature a wide variety of events, from popular sporting matches to global events like elections, award shows, or financial outcomes.
    
3.  **Place Your Bet:** After selecting an event, choose the participant or outcome you want to back. For example, in the US Elections 2024, you might choose to bet on either Donald Trump or Kamala Harris. Enter your stake (the amount of your bet).
    
4.  **Time of Bet Placement:** The time at which you place your bet plays a crucial role in determining your potential bonus. The earlier you place your bet, the higher the bonus you’ll receive if your prediction turns out correct. This encourages placing bets as soon as possible to maximize returns.
    
5.  **Monitor your bets:** You can see all your open bets in the "My Bets" tab on the bottom of the page.
    

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/events#decision)

Decision


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Each event has a set deadline for determining a winner and paying out rewards. The payout time is listed in each event’s terms & conditions, and a countdown to payout is displayed for all completed events. If, for any reason, the event isn’t decided by then, Betfin will refund the bets. The decision is made by the decision wallet.

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/events#payout-structure)

Payout Structure


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The payout for winning bets is calculated based on:

• **Stake Amount:** Your reward is proportional to your stake. The larger your bet, the bigger your share of the total prize pool.

• **Bet Placement Time:** Early birds get rewarded! Bets placed earlier receive a higher bonus compared to those placed closer to the event’s conclusion.

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/events#strategy-tips)

Strategy tips


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Bet early**: Secure the maximum possible bonus by betting early. Let’s say you bet on Donald Trump three months before the election, while another player bets on him one week before the election. If Trump wins, both players win, but the first player will receive a significantly higher bonus because they placed their bet earlier.
    
*   **Stay informed:** Follow real-time updates about events to make more informed bets.
    

[PreviousLURO Terms](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/lucky-round-luro/luro-terms)
[NextEvents T&C](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/events/events-t-and-c)

Last updated 9 months ago

# Stones | GAMES MANUAL | BETFIN DOCS

![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1825326731-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSinPZEOuPy8TM9anY3n8%252Fuploads%252F8S0Ow0Abt5cYrcEhKHaQ%252FScreenshot%25202024-11-19%2520at%252012.49.21.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0efcb1f7-9b7b-4343-8143-0f2fcc7ea418&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ea213d76&sv=2)

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/stones#how-the-game-works)

How the Game Works


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In the Stones you can choose one of the five stones. The wheel spins every 5 minutes and the winning stone is drawn.

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/stones#game-logic)

Game Logic


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Each stone has its own multiplier based on how much of the pool it takes up. The smaller its share, the bigger the payout. This means the less popular stones can win you more, adding extra excitement to your picks!

![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1825326731-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSinPZEOuPy8TM9anY3n8%252Fuploads%252FeQ8DPJXPYbor55qlkBKb%252FScreenshot%25202024-12-10%2520at%252015.58.14.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1c1216e9-02fd-4465-a260-5f140b09c00c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d2af9ced&sv=2)

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/stones#how-to-bet)

How to Bet


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Connect Wallet**: Connect your wallet to Betfin.
    
2.  **Select a stone:** Choose one the five stones. You can see which stones are other users are betting on and what is the winning percentage and potentional winning.
    
3.  **Enter the Betting Amount:** After selecting the stone, enter the betting amount.
    
4.  **Time of Bet Placement:** The time at which you place your bet plays a crucial role in determining your potential bonus. The earlier you place your bet, the higher the bonus you’ll receive if your prediction turns out correct. This encourages placing bets as soon as possible to maximize returns.
    
5.  **Monitor your bets:** You can see all your open bets in the "My Bets" tab on the bottom of the page.
    
6.  **Resolution:** The wheel will spin a few seconds after the countdown is over.
    

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/stones#winner-announcement)

Winner Announcement


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **End of Round**: Once the 5-minute countdown is over no further bets are accepted.
    
2.  **Random Selection**: The system randomly selects the winning stone. This selection is transparent and recorded on the blockchain. The winner (or winners) is announced as soon as the random number is received from Chainlink VRF.
    
3.  **Winner Notification**: The winners are notified, and 95% of all bets from that round are automatically transferred to their account. The remaining 5% is distributed as a bonus. Additionally, 3.6% of the winnings are allocated to conservative staking.
    
4.  **The winning amount:** The winning amount is calculated in proportion to the bet amounts.
    

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/stones#bonus)

Bonus


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Allocation**: 5% of all bets in a round go into the bonus pool.
    
*   **Logic**: The bonus is split based on the size and order of the bets. The first bet out of 10 gets an order coefficient of 10, and the last one gets a coefficient of 1. The size coefficient matches the bet amount.
    
*   Bonus is added to your winning automatically. You do not need to claim it.
    

[PreviousEvents T&C](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/events/events-t-and-c)
[NextStones T&C](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/stones/stones-t-and-c)

# Chainlink & Datafeeds | GAMES MANUAL | BETFIN DOCS

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/proof-of-fairness/chainlink-and-datafeeds#overview)

**Overview**

Chainlink datafeeds ensure Betfin.io's decentralized games receive reliable and tamper-proof price data, maintaining the integrity and fairness of financial and prediction games.

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/proof-of-fairness/chainlink-and-datafeeds#reliable-price-data)

**Reliable Price Data**

*   **High-Quality Sources:** Data is gathered from premium and verified providers.
    
*   **Decentralized Oracles:** Multiple independent oracles aggregate the data to ensure accuracy.
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/proof-of-fairness/chainlink-and-datafeeds#how-it-works)

**How It Works**

1.  **Data Aggregation:** Chainlink oracles collect data from numerous reliable sources.
    
2.  **Data Transmission:** The aggregated data is securely transmitted to Betfin.io's smart contracts.
    
3.  **Data Utilization:** Betfin.io uses this data for game outcomes and financial predictions.
    

![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1825326731-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSinPZEOuPy8TM9anY3n8%252Fuploads%252F71ydCPeqTMsRIfFpDYsV%252FScreenshot%25202024-02-03%2520at%252019.22.12.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5897c5c8-f25d-4fc1-b46f-0ac5fb60dd2b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=42db3be0&sv=2)

This is the example of BTC/USD datafeed on [https://data.chain.link/feeds/polygon/mainnet/btc-usd#operator-linkforest](https://data.chain.link/feeds/polygon/mainnet/btc-usd#operator-linkforest)

# Random Number Generation | GAMES MANUAL | BETFIN DOCS

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/proof-of-fairness/random-number-generation#chainlink-vrf-verifiable-random-function)

**Chainlink VRF (Verifiable Random Function)**

Chainlink VRF provides a secure and verifiable method for generating random numbers, ensuring that game outcomes are fair and tamper-proof.

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/proof-of-fairness/random-number-generation#how-it-works)

**How It Works**

1.  **Request for Randomness:** Betfin.io's smart contract requests a random number from Chainlink VRF.
    
2.  **VRF Process:** A Chainlink node generates a random number along with a cryptographic proof.
    
3.  **Verification:** The smart contract verifies the proof before using the random number in game outcomes.
    

Decentralized generation of random number is the only fair way

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/proof-of-fairness/random-number-generation#integration)

Integration

*   Each dynamic game that is connected to dynamic staking have implemented the chainlink VRF
    
*   You can verify the random number generation by yourself in transaction logs!
    

![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1825326731-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSinPZEOuPy8TM9anY3n8%252Fuploads%252F6jtTZhOf72eUIA84npTh%252FScreenshot%25202024-05-12%2520at%252014.03.32.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D74becb3b-f11c-4349-aa62-71982ec4662d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a8292f8e&sv=2)

Check the detail of your past bet

![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1825326731-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSinPZEOuPy8TM9anY3n8%252Fuploads%252Fuqo1abZTLNMUnp6rTpaq%252FScreenshot%25202024-05-12%2520at%252014.05.26.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfb0cd8b8-9e20-4782-beb6-5213c11d0fa4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2e4401cc&sv=2)

See the number that was generated in trasanction logs from chainlink

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/proof-of-fairness/random-number-generation#benefits)

**Benefits**

*   **Security:** Cryptographic proof ensures results are not manipulated.
    
*   **Transparency:** Users can independently verify the fairness of game outcomes.
    
*   **Decentralization:** Chainlink's decentralized oracle network ensures that no single entity controls the random number generation process.
    

[PreviousChainlink & Datafeeds](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/proof-of-fairness/chainlink-and-datafeeds)
