# Lotto | GAMES MANUAL | BETFIN DOCS

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/lotto#how-the-lotto-works-basics)

**How the lotto Works (basics)**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   In Lotto, you select **5 numbers per line** from a range of **1 to 25**.
    
*   Purchasing at least **3 lines activates a special symbol**, which is essential for superjackpot eligibility.
    
*   To win the **SUPERJACKPOT**, you must correctly match all **5 numbers + symbol** and have the symbol activated (3lines or more in single ticket)
    

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/lotto#how-to-play-the-lotto)

How to play the lotto


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/lotto#paytable-if-ticket-price-is-1-500-bet)

Paytable (if ticket price is 1,500 BET)


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   See the detailed table in [Lotto T&C](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/lotto/lotto-t-and-c)
    

![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1825326731-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSinPZEOuPy8TM9anY3n8%252Fuploads%252FZNGICYsva6auoX1Gqujr%252FScreenshot%25202025-03-25%2520at%252017.58.15.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0e1f1143-bdd0-41a3-b419-0dfc209c54cc&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2664d676&sv=2)

_It is simple. The more lines you have, the bigger the chance to win! We recommend the minimum of three lines per ticket to be eligible for the SUPERJACKPOT._

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/lotto#draw-schedule)

Draw Schedule


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

• Lotto draws take place twice a week, on Tuesday and Friday.

• Each ticket can be purchased for one or multiple draws in advance.

• There is an option to buy a ticket for someone else and send it as a gift.

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/lotto#winner-announcement)

Winner Announcement


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once the countdown is over, Chainlink randomly selects winning numbers and symbol (everything is transparent and stored on blockchain, link is provided in each draw detail page). From this moment your ticket can be found in a section Old tickets. Each ticket in this section has one of the following labels:

*   WON (Claim button will appear and you can claim our winnings)
    
*   LOST
    
*   WAITING (You need to wait for the status to change and Claim button to appear)
    

By clicking on a particular draw in a All Draws section on the bottom of the pages, you will directing to the draw detail. This is where you can find draw details such us:

*   drawn numbers and symbol
    
*   total number of lines that participaed
    
*   total BET amount spend
    
*   total amount that was paid to the Dynamic staking
    
*   overview of all your tickets that were in this draw
    

![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1825326731-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSinPZEOuPy8TM9anY3n8%252Fuploads%252FvEnZLdWCkSLJ6iAkA9ar%252FScreenshot%25202025-03-25%2520at%252019.49.28.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da6c34149-368b-4943-a7a5-d57440b2110c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1bd70d9&sv=2)

*   further down you can find a table containing all winning tickets and total amounts that were paid out:
    

![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1825326731-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSinPZEOuPy8TM9anY3n8%252Fuploads%252FkziMnpWSgwxDnZis7VXL%252FScreenshot%25202025-03-25%2520at%252019.49.39.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7de42888-baf5-44d2-83b7-1d25020f7dbb&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=64db8d18&sv=2)

The Link to Proof of randomness is on the bottom of each draw detail.

The contract is audited by CertiK and Ackee.

All proceeds from the Lotto game are subject of Dynamic staking.

SuperJackpot Bonus

*   Represents 4% of all bets placed since the last superjackpot was won
    
*   SuperJacpot bonus is won only if superjacpot is hit otherwise is cummulated in the main lotto contract
    
*   There is no limit for the size of the superjackpot

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/lotto/lotto-t-and-c#fallback-time)

Fallback time

*   3hours
    
*   If there is not enough funds on dynamic staking within 3 hours since draw time the draw is cancelled
    
*   Dynamic staking has payout limit of 5% on a single round

# Lotto Round & Winners Protection | GAMES MANUAL | BETFIN DOCS

Each bet that is placed into lotto game has two possible scenarios - lost of bet or winning payout and return of the bet. You may say: _**How can I be sure that promised payout will be paid to me**_? Well, Betfin has a unique system of winners protection that covers each winnings even before the lotto has started!

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/proof-of-fairness/lotto-round-and-winners-protection#round-process)

**Round process**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Before the bet is placed betfin contract verifies if there is enough BET reserve for payout in case of wining and if such winning doesn't treat the dynamic staking pool
    
    *   Betfin has its own mechanism that decides if bet can be accepted or not
        
    
*   When member spins the game the potential winning is transferred from Dynamic staking to so-called winners protection pool which is held by the contract of the lotto game.
    
    *   **Therefore user can be 100% sure that his winning is protected!**
        
        *   (photo)
            
        
    

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/proof-of-fairness/lotto-round-and-winners-protection#dynamic-games-result-execution)

**Dynamic games result execution**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   In case that the bet is lost the full bet amount of bet and the potential winning is transferred from the lotto game contract into to dynamic staking. That means dynamic pool earned the 100% of the bet size.
    
*   In case that there is a win the game contract executes the booked winning directly to user.
    

[PreviousRandom Number Generation](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/proof-of-fairness/random-number-generation)
[NextGeneral Strategy](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-strategies/general-strategy)

# Roulette | GAMES MANUAL | BETFIN DOCS

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/roulette#introduction)

**Introduction**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

_Roulette is a classic casino game where players bet on where a ball will land on a spinning wheel. Betfin.io offers a decentralized version of this game using blockchain technology for transparency and fairness._

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/roulette#how-it-works)

**How It Works**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Bet Placement:** Players place bets on various outcomes (e.g., single number, color, odd/even).
    
2.  **Spin:** The wheel spins, and a random number is generated using a secure, verifiable random function.
    
3.  **Outcome:** If the ball lands on a number that matches the bet, the player wins based on the payout odds.
    

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/roulette#bet-types-and-payouts)

**Bet Types and Payouts**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Single Number (Straight):** 35 to 1
    
*   **Two Numbers (Split):** 17 to 1
    
*   **Three Numbers (Street):** 11 to 1
    
*   **Four Numbers (Corner):** 8 to 1
    
*   **Six Numbers (Line):** 5 to 1
    
*   **Column/Dozen:** 2 to 1
    
*   **Red/Black, Even/Odd, High/Low:** 1 to 1
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/roulette#fairness)

**Fairness**

*   Betfin.io uses blockchain and Gelato technology for random number generator and fair results.
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/roulette#strategy)

**Strategy**

*   Understand betting strategies and manage your bankroll wisely for better outcomes.
    

For a more detailed explanation, visit the [Roulette Explanation](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-guide/roulette-single-player/roulette-explanation)
 page.

![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1825326731-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSinPZEOuPy8TM9anY3n8%252Fuploads%252FfsxaCJpz7KM0zbjT6Zlk%252FScreenshot%25202024-04-28%2520at%252016.25.12.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D334a1a1a-d379-4720-90b6-393c4339e88a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f52cdf04&sv=2)

BetFin roulette screenshot

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/roulette#remember-that)

Remember that


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   BetFin roulette is not a standard casino game where you bet against the platfrom.
    
*   BetFin roulette is a smart contract that allows you to place your bet against other users that stakes their bet tokens in dynamic contract.
    
*   The process of the games which means generation of random number, decision wether you win and payout is proceed automatically without control of anyone.
    
*   This logic is common for all lotto games.
    

**Link for betfin roulette here:** [**https://betfin.io/roulette**](https://betfin.io/roulette)

# General Strategy | GAMES MANUAL | BETFIN DOCS

![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1825326731-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSinPZEOuPy8TM9anY3n8%252Fuploads%252FCOs58YRWeq9Duj5hW18e%252FScreenshot%25202024-04-28%2520at%252016.19.34.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D26f84ffb-4f2e-48d3-9dc2-5ecfef6caf1e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6f008d0d&sv=2)

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-strategies/general-strategy#be-responsible)

**Be Responsible**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Play for entertainment and without excess.
    
*   If you find that the game is starting to affect you emotionally or financially, take a break or stop.
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-strategies/general-strategy#set-a-budget)

**Set a Budget**

*   Establish the amount of money you are willing to spend on playing games and stick to that budget.
    
*   Never wager more than you can afford to lose.
    
*   You can set this up by caping your allowance or not transfering BET tokens on your wallet
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-strategies/general-strategy#manage-your-time)

**Manage Your Time**

*   Set a time limit for your gaming session and adhere to it.
    
*   After the designated time has elapsed, assess your experience and decide whether to continue or end your gameplay.
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-strategies/general-strategy#diversify-your-play)

**Diversify Your Play**

*   Experiment with different games to diversify your experience and avoid monotony.
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-strategies/general-strategy#remember-the-element-of-chance)

**Remember the Element of Chance**

*   Keep in mind that the outcome of each spin in lotto games is entirely random, and previous results do not influence future ones.
    
*   Don't attempt to develop a system to "beat" the game.
    

[PreviousLotto Round & Winners Protection](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/proof-of-fairness/lotto-round-and-winners-protection)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Conservative vs Dynamic Games | GAMES MANUAL | BETFIN DOCS

![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1825326731-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSinPZEOuPy8TM9anY3n8%252Fuploads%252FCOs58YRWeq9Duj5hW18e%252FScreenshot%25202024-04-28%2520at%252016.19.34.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D26f84ffb-4f2e-48d3-9dc2-5ecfef6caf1e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6f008d0d&sv=2)

Logic aspects of Conservative games

Logic aspects of Dynamic games

*   Each game has round with time countdown (however rounds with countdown can be also subject of some lotto games)
    
*   Round result is defined by the result of certain event that can be either random or comming out of the real world.
    
*   Bet payout is coming out of other bets in the round
    
*   There is no limit for the maximum bet
    
*   The payout rate is defined by the ratio between the bets
    
*   It is not possible to play alone without other players being live on the platform as the payout
    
*   Winning is a subject of winning fee that supports [Conservative Staking Manual](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-user-manual/conservative-staking-manual)
    

*   Bet payout is comming out of the bank that is created by the [Dynamic Staking Manual](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-user-manual/dynamic-staking-manual)
    
*   Payout always depends on the random event
    
*   Odds for each combination are pre-defined and unchangeable
    
*   There are limits of minimal and maximal bet per each combination
    
*   It is possible to play the round alone without others but there can be also live game
    
*   There is not a winning fee but each game has certain RTP (return to players) coefficient that gives players slightly higher probability of loosing than winning in the long run.
    

*   Split of games for conservative games and dynamic games is visible in the menu of this GAMES MANUAL
    
*   Connection of games to staking system is visible in [Staking revenue model](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/staking-manual/staking-explanation/staking-revenue-model)
    

[PreviousGames FAQ](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-guide/games-faq)
[NextGAMES TERMS & CONDITIONS](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/games-manual/games-terms/games-terms-and-conditions)

Last updated 9 months ago

# BET Token | BETFIN DOCS

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/tokenomy/bet-token#about-bet-token)

#About BET token


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

BET is the native token of the Betfin ecosystem. BET is a pure utility token that is used for all possible transactions within the ecosystem such as:

*   Staking to any possible staking and its payouts.
    
*   Betting to any game and its payouts.
    
*   Payout of affiliate bonuses.
    
*   Payout of partner profits.
    

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/tokenomy/bet-token#bet-token-technical-fact-sheet)

**BET token technical fact sheet:**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Fact

Detail

Note

Chain

EVM: Polygon POS

No other chains yet

Token address

[0xbf7970d56a150cd0b60bd08388a4a75a27777777](https://polygonscan.com/token/0xbf7970d56a150cd0b60bd08388a4a75a27777777)

[Open-sourced](https://polygonscan.com/token/0xbf7970d56a150cd0b60bd08388a4a75a27777777#code)

Total supply

777,777,777,777 BET

[BET initial distribution](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/tokenomy/bet-initial-distribution)

Number of decimals

18

\-

PAUSE function

no

Contract can not be paused

FREEZE function

no

No transaction can be frozen

MINT function

no

Supply can not be increased

Burn or tax mechanism

no

There is no burn or tax

Access control

none

Issuer has no special rights

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/tokenomy/bet-token#bet-tokens-utility-and-value)

BET token's utility and value


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   _BET token is not backed by any asset such as share, commodities, FIAT money or centrally managed value._
    
*   _BET token does not guarantee or generate any returns_
    
*   BET token does not have any initial, minimal or maximal value
    
*   BET token price is result of demand and supply on free market.
    
*   _BET token is the only unit that gives you access to Betfin smart contracts._
    
*   _BET token demand is based on the demanded for the Betfin technology._

# Team Pool | BETFIN DOCS

The team pool includes 18% of all tokens (140B BET tokens) that are dedicated to the core team members such as responsible executives, developers and project managers.

As the project is decentralized the team tokens are the key motivation for the team members to invest their time, finance and energy to the project.

Team tokens are dedicated in a special vesting contract with the following terms:

**The team agreed to set a vesting of 5 years that would start 3 years after the project launch.**

*   After 3 years 7B (7,000,000,000) BET tokens will be unlocked each quarter for 5 years.
    
*   That means the internal team will not be able to sell any tokens within the first 3 years.
    
*   The full exit of team tokens will not be possible earlier than in 8 years since **1st June 2024**
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/tokenomy/bet-initial-distribution/team-pool#verify-team-pool-and-its-ownership)

Verify team pool and its ownership

# Buy BET token | BETFIN DOCS

Currently, the following options are available for buying and selling the BET token:

Have crypto - buy on uniswap

Don't have crypto - buy it

If you are familiar with trading crypto onchain, its very simple:

*   Transfer crypto to your web3 wallet on Polygon mainnet
    
*   Visit the [https://app.uniswap.org/swap](https://app.uniswap.org/swap)
    
*   Connect your wallet to Uniswap
    
*   Be sure you are using uniswap on Polygon mainnet
    
*   Ensure you left some cryptocurrency POL to execute the transaction (and also future ones)
    
*   Select the token or cryptocurrency you want to swap, and for the token you want to buy, select BET token
    
    *   If you have trouble to find BET you can find it by using this contract address: 0xbF7970D56a150cD0b60BD08388A4A75a27777777 (address must fully match!)
        
    
*   Sign the message and execute the swap. BET tokens should arrive within a few seconds.
    

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/tokenomy/bet-token/buy-bet-token#what-crypto-to-buy)

What crypto to buy?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   We recommend purchasing MATIC tokens, as you will need them to pay for transaction fees later.
    
*   We don't recommend swapping 100% of your MATIC for BET, as you won't be able to stake or place bets without MATIC for fees.
    
*   If you plan to make regular purchases, consider buying USDT or USDC, **but make sure they are on the Polygon network.**
    

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/tokenomy/bet-token/buy-bet-token#where-to-buy-crypto)

Where to buy crypto


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   _Setup bank account with_ card _on Revolut app that is available for apple and_ android
    
*   _Use cex exchanges such as binance, bybit or mexc.com_
    
*   _Buy crypto P2P from community (be always cautious on P2P transactions to maintain security and legal risks)_
    
*   _Use onramp solutions such as transak.com, guardarian.com or others_
    
*   Use alternative exchange options available on [www.bestchange.com](https://www.bestchange.com/)
    

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/tokenomy/bet-token/buy-bet-token#important-tips)

Important Tips:


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Network Fees**: Be aware of transaction (gas) fees on the Polygon network. You will need some MATIC in your wallet to cover these fees.
    
*   **Slippage**: Adjust the slippage tolerance if necessary, especially during periods of high volatility.
    
*   **Double-Check Addresses**: Always ensure you are using the correct contract address for the BET token.
    
*   **Security**: Use caution and ensure that you are interacting with the official Uniswap interface.
    

[PreviousBET Token](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/tokenomy/bet-token)
[NextBET initial distribution](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/tokenomy/bet-initial-distribution)

Last updated 9 months ago

# Timelock Principle | BETFIN DOCS

Timelock is another mechanism of BET token holders' protection. Timelock gives users space to prepare for the change that was confirmed by a quorum of owners based on

Technically each contract is executed by timelock.

Betfin timelock conditions:

*   Betfin has only one timelock principle for all contract-related transactions.
    
*   After the quorum signs certain transactions then there is 24 24-hour period when the transaction is waiting to inform the community.
    
*   After that 24 hours of waiting time, there is 72 hours of space to execute the transaction.
    

[PreviousBetfin governance](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/betfin-governance/betfin-governance)
[NextMultisignature (multisig) Principle](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/betfin-governance/betfin-governance/multisignature-multisig-principle)

# Tokenomy FAQ | BETFIN DOCS

Where can I buy or sell a BET token?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/tokenomy/tokenomy-faq#where-can-i-buy-or-sell-a-bet-token)

You can purchase BET through uniswap.com for any tradable token.

What is a BET token and how is it connected to Betfin?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/tokenomy/tokenomy-faq#what-is-a-bet-token-and-how-is-it-connected-to-betfin)

BET is a utility token of betfin platform. All transactions on the Betfin platform are settled only in BET token. That brings the BET token its utility.

Why does the BET token have a value and how is it derived?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/tokenomy/tokenomy-faq#why-does-the-bet-token-have-a-value-and-how-is-it-derived)

BET token has value because there is a supply that is generated by users who want to use the Betfin technology.

Price is derived only by demand and supply and there is no central entity that controls or backs the BET token's price

Are BET and stakers holders protected against rugpull or team dump?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/tokenomy/tokenomy-faq#are-bet-and-stakers-holders-protected-against-rugpull-or-team-dump)

**Yes**, there are protection mechanisms tha technically guarantess that developers or initial airdrop holder con not dump tokens and run away. The mechanisms are following:

*   [Community lockup](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/tokenomy/liquidity-and-lockups/community-lockup)
    of initial airdrop winners
    
*   [Team Pool](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/tokenomy/bet-initial-distribution/team-pool)
    vesting is set for 5 years starting after 3 years since the project launched.
    
*   [Team.finance lockups](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/tokenomy/liquidity-and-lockups/team.finance-lockups)
    

Is't BET a security token?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/tokenomy/tokenomy-faq#ist-bet-a-security-token)

BET token itself has no security function as it does not represent and is not backed by any asset, service or value. Its value is fully created by community demand. Moreover BET token was never subject initial public token sale such as IEO and is not even listed on any centralized exchange.

What chains are supported by Betfin?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/tokenomy/tokenomy-faq#what-chains-are-supported-by-betfin)

BetFin currently runs on Polygon. Network name: Polygon Mainnet. RPC URL: https://polygon-rpc.com. Chain ID: 137. There are no official wrapped versions on other chans.

Why does the BET token exist?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/tokenomy/tokenomy-faq#why-does-the-bet-token-exist)

BET token is here to allow Betfin technology fast expansion as third party issued asset would require significant investment of initial value while creation of unique asset which empowers the technology allows the value creation thanks to the community demand.

[PreviousTeam.finance lockups](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/tokenomy/liquidity-and-lockups/team.finance-lockups)
[NextBetfin Contract Addresses](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/betfin-governance/betfin-contract-addresses)

Last updated 9 months ago

# Community lockup | BETFIN DOCS

*   Initial airdrop contest winners could claim a share on the liquidity reward pool of 4,490,416,666 BET as a renumeration for locking their Uniswap liquidity into community lockup contract.
    
*   Share on the reward pool of particular user was set based on lockup range height, duration and size of the lockup. Reward pool share can be claimed after the end of the lockup period!
    
*   Community lockup contract address: [0xBFDd7f3E2cB6976BbAc395E3A79aA4274ECccccC](https://polygonscan.com/address/0xBFDd7f3E2cB6976BbAc395E3A79aA4274ECccccC#nfttransfers)

# Partners Pool | BETFIN DOCS

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/tokenomy/bet-initial-distribution/partners-pool#what-is-it)

What is it?


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The partners pool is the motivation of Partners to bring users to games and staking in different platforms and markets. Partners are remunerated according to their [Partner Tariff Terms](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/for-partners/faq-and-terms/partner-tariff-terms)
 from partner pool for the following transactions:

*   Stake to dynamic or conservative staking
    
*   Bet to the lotto games (dynamic games)
    

_In case of conservative games, the partners are paid directly from the winning fees._

**To understand this we recommend to read** [Partner Contract Explained](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/for-partners/about-partner-contract/partner-contract-explained)

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/tokenomy/bet-initial-distribution/partners-pool#more-information-about-partners-pool)

**More information about partners pool:**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Partners pool has no vesting as tokens have to be available just in time when the partner brings the user to the game and to staking.
    
*   Partners pool is held in the [Core](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/core)
    contract as the partner claims its revenue directly from there.
    
*   The 6% from total emission (46.66B BET tokens) that is on the core contract can not be withdrawn by any party
    
    *   The only option how to get those tokens into circulation is when Partner brings a new volume to games or new stakers.
        
    *   Each unlock of partners tokens brings new demand to the market. Therefore we can say that those tokens are backed by business.
        
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/tokenomy/bet-initial-distribution/partners-pool#verify-the-pool)

Verify the pool

*   Partner's pool is the CORE contract.
    
*   Consensus and ownership of the core contract can be verified in [Betfin governance](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/betfin-governance/betfin-governance)
    
*   Core contract link: [here](https://polygonscan.com/address/0xbf87898c4e609598a393ccd765482bef80000000#code)
    

[PreviousTeam Pool](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/tokenomy/bet-initial-distribution/team-pool)
[NextAirdrop Pool](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/tokenomy/bet-initial-distribution/airdrop-pool)

# Airdrop Pool | BETFIN DOCS

The Airdrop pool represents 21% of total BET emission (163.33B BET tokens). The Airdrop pool is split into 3 main sub-allocations:

Airdrop pool allocation

Share on airdrop pool

Nominal allocation

Initial airdrop phase 1

21%

34,300,000,000 BET

Initial airdrop phase 2

73,5%

120,050,000,000 BET

Secondary airdrop

5,5%

8,983,333,333 BET

![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F165088273-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrHOKQrd3to9xOScdSF8N%252Fuploads%252F5WDQ9qlIddfY2bJ65zqx%252FScreenshot%25202024-04-26%2520at%252018.33.46.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da2d279da-f589-4847-921f-f3a4d668e772&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=555e0fac&sv=2)

Initial airdrop distribution

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/tokenomy/bet-initial-distribution/airdrop-pool#initial-airdrop-pool-phase-1)

**Initial Airdrop Pool Phase 1**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   First phase of initial airdrop is available for limited amount of 25,000 early project adopters
    
*   Each user should receive 1,372,000 BET token upon accepted registration
    
*   Registration for initial airdrop event is available [HERE](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/about-betfin-1/tokenomy/bet-initial-distribution/airdrop-pool/initial-airdrop-and-predict-contest)
    

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/tokenomy/bet-initial-distribution/airdrop-pool#initial-airdrop-pool-phase-2-predict-contest)

**Initial Airdrop Pool Phase 2 (predict contest)**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Participants of phase 1 will be the first owners of Betfin PASS - access to Predict contest
    
*   Predict contest is very simple: earn as much tokens as possible on Predict game within 10 days
    
*   Second airdrop tranche will be distributed based on final balances in the end of the predict contest
    
    *   The size of the second tranche will be 3.5 times bigger than the first tranche in total
        
    *   Your particular airdrop size may vary according to your final outstanding balance
        
    *   Rewards generated by conservative staking are counted as Predict contest results!
        
    

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/tokenomy/bet-initial-distribution/airdrop-pool#secondary-airdrop-community-lockup-and-multiple-pools-liquidity)

Secondary airdrop - community lockup & multiple pools liquidity


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   This event aims to get the biggest liquidity locked in Uniswap V3
    
*   50% or this allocation (4,490,416,666 BET) is a renumeration of predict contest winners for locking the won tokens as a liquidity in uniswap.
    
    *   Result of this event to be found in [Community lockup](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/tokenomy/liquidity-and-lockups/community-lockup)
        
    
*   Second half (4,490,416,666 BET) is being swapped for major cryptocurencies via Uniswap and being supplied as a liquidity in the full range!
    
    *   See the currently available pools and liquidity in [betfin stats](https://betfin.io/statistics)
         or in [Liquidity and lockups](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/tokenomy/liquidity-and-lockups)
        
    

[PreviousPartners Pool](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/tokenomy/bet-initial-distribution/partners-pool)

# BET initial distribution | BETFIN DOCS

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/tokenomy/bet-initial-distribution#philosophy-of-betfin-tokenomics)

Philosophy of Betfin Tokenomics


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**There is a limited total supply of 777,777,777,777 BET tokens.**

*   _The total supply is 100% pre-minted but can never be increased!_
    
*   _**The majority**_ _of tokens is_ _**not in circulation**_ _since the very beginning and was transferred to smart-contracts which manages tokens_ _**unlock process to protect holders**__._
    
*   _Innovative unlock mechanism and contract utility model brings long-term sustainable tokenomy_
    
*   _Team tokens will unlock on the last place_
    

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/tokenomy/bet-initial-distribution#initial-bet-token-distribution)

Initial BET Token Distribution


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

# Multisignature (multisig) Principle | BETFIN DOCS

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/betfin-governance/betfin-governance/multisignature-multisig-principle#what-is-the-multisignature-principle)

What is the Multisignature Principle


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To maximise the protection and security Betfin implemented the multisignature consensus. That means that every important transaction is done by more than one signatory. This proceeds through [**safe.global**](https://safe.global/)
 multisig contract.

*   Timelock contract (see [Timelock Principle](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/betfin-governance/betfin-governance/timelock-principle)
    ) which owns all the Betfin contracts is owned by multisignature contract.
    
*   Multisignature contract has a quorum of 5 wallets where 3 out of 5 has to sign each transaction.
    
*   To see the quorum of multisignature wallets that own the Betfin contracts check.
    
*   Betfin uses a multisignature wallet provided by safe.global.
    
    *   [https://safe.global/](https://safe.global/)
         is the world's leading and most trusted provider of multisignature wallets.
        
    *   All the Betfin on-chain confirmations and rejections can be verified at [https://polygonscan.com/](https://polygonscan.com/)
         and [https://app.safe.global/](https://app.safe.global/transactions/history?safe=matic:0xAD0b2Ade32Bb9FC701ba966fDb7DeC286265e1Be)
        .
        
    

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/betfin-governance/betfin-governance/multisignature-multisig-principle#transaction-types-that-are-subject-to-the-multisignature-principle)

**Transaction types that are subject to the Multisignature principle**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Token transfers from any of the that allow it.
    
2.  Any transaction related to the Betfin contract such as: - adding new game - changing the minimums or maximum bets in games, - changing limits in staking - changing the limits of affiliate - Any other change that is possible concerning the settings of
    
3.  Change in the quorum of any of [Betfin governance](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/betfin-governance/betfin-governance)
    

Moreover, any transaction that is signed by the last needed owner of the multisignature wallet is subject to [Timelock Principle](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/betfin-governance/betfin-governance/timelock-principle)
.

[PreviousTimelock Principle](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/betfin-governance/betfin-governance/timelock-principle)
[NextInternal Wallets & External Contracts](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/betfin-governance/internal-wallets-and-external-contracts)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Smart Contract Template | BETFIN DOCS

All smart contracts are located in [https://github.com/betfinio/shared](https://github.com/betfinio/shared)
 among with their deployed version on Polygon Network.

The most important contract is Core.sol which is entry point for any bet or stake.

Your new game must be based on GameInterface.sol and implement all functions.

Feel free to get inspiration from Predict game or any other to create new games. Use the [Web Template](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/for-developers/web-template)
 to implement Web Interface for your game to be easily integrated to existing environment.

Once tested and deployed on testnet(Polygon Amoy - 80002), reach us to get your game deployed on mainnet. Prepare you source code repository on github.com, that must be public!

[PreviousWeb Template](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/for-developers/web-template)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Tariff | BETFIN DOCS

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/core/tariff#overview)

Overview

The Tariff contract defines the pricing and profit distribution parameters for partners within the ecosystem. It specifies the amount of tokens required as payment for creating a Partner, the percentage of each bet that the partner will receive as profit, and the percentage of each stake that the partner will receive as profit.

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/core/tariff#contract-structure)

Contract Structure

The Tariff contract consists of immutable variables to define the pricing and profit parameters.

#### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/core/tariff#constructor)

Constructor

`**constructor**`: Initializes the Tariff contract with the specified price, profit percentage for bets, and profit percentage for stakes.

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/core/tariff#variables)

Variables

`**price**`: Amount of BET tokens required as payment for creating a partner

`**profit**`: Percentage of each bet that the partner will receive as profit (ranging from 0% to 3.60%).

`**stakeProfit**`: Percentage of each stake that the partner will receive as profit (ranging from 0% to 100%).

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/core/tariff#dependencies)

Dependencies

The Tariff contract operates independently and does not have explicit dependencies on other contracts within the ecosystem.

[PreviousPartner](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/core/partner)
[NextConservative Staking](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/conservative-staking)

Last updated 1 year ago

---

# Conservative Staking Pool | BETFIN DOCS

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/conservative-staking/conservative-staking-pool#overview)

Overview

The Conservative Staking Pool contract implements a staking pool where users can stake tokens for a specified duration. It provides functionalities for staking tokens, claiming rewards, withdrawing stakes, and distributing profits among stakers.

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/conservative-staking/conservative-staking-pool#contract-structure)

Contract Structure

The Conservative Staking Pool contract utilizes AccessControl and ReentrancyGuard from OpenZeppelin for access control and protection against reentrancy attacks.

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/conservative-staking/conservative-staking-pool#variables)

Variables

*   `duration`: Duration of the staking pool.
    
*   `token`: ERC20 token contract address.
    
*   `totalStaked`: Total amount of tokens staked in the pool.
    
*   `totalProfit`: Total profit earned by stakers.
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/conservative-staking/conservative-staking-pool#functions)

Functions

*   `stake`: Allows users to stake tokens in the pool.
    
*   `claim`: Allows stakers to claim their rewards.
    
*   `withdraw`: Allows stakers to withdraw their stakes after the staking duration ends.
    
*   `distributeProfit`: Distributes profits among stakers in the pool.
    

[PreviousConservative Staking](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/conservative-staking)
[NextDynamic Staking](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/dynamic-staking)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Bet Interface | BETFIN DOCS

The Bet Interface provides methods to interact with a betting contract on the Ethereum blockchain. This interface allows users to retrieve various information related to a bet, such as player address, bet amount, payout result, bet status, game address, and creation timestamp.

#### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/bet-interface#interface-methods)

Interface Methods

1.  **getPlayer**
    
    *   **Description**: Returns the address of the player who placed the bet.
        
    *   **Usage**: Call this method to retrieve the address of the player.
        
    *   **Return Type**: `address`
        
    
2.  **getAmount**
    
    *   **Description**: Returns the amount of the bet.
        
    *   **Usage**: Call this method to retrieve the amount of the bet in Wei.
        
    *   **Return Type**: `uint256`
        
    
3.  **getResult**
    
    *   **Description**: Returns the payout result of the bet.
        
    *   **Usage**: Call this method to retrieve the payout result of the bet.
        
    *   **Return Type**: `uint256`
        
    
4.  **getStatus**
    
    *   **Description**: Returns the status of the bet.
        
    *   **Usage**: Call this method to retrieve the status of the bet.
        
    *   **Return Type**: `uint256`
        
    
5.  **getGame**
    
    *   **Description**: Returns the address of the game associated with the bet.
        
    *   **Usage**: Call this method to retrieve the address of the game contract.
        
    *   **Return Type**: `address`
        
    
6.  **getCreated**
    
    *   **Description**: Returns the timestamp when the bet was created.
        
    *   **Usage**: Call this method to retrieve the creation timestamp of the bet.
        
    *   **Return Type**: `uint256`
        
    
7.  **getBetInfo**
    
    *   **Description**: Returns all relevant information about the bet.
        
    *   **Usage**: Call this method to retrieve all data related to the bet at once, including player address, game address, bet amount, payout result, bet status, and creation timestamp.
        
    *   **Return Type**: `(address, address, uint256, uint256, uint256, uint256)`
        
    

[PreviousGame Interface](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/game-interface)
[NextPredict Contract](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/predict-contract)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Bonus Pool | BETFIN DOCS

The Bonus Pool contains 6% (46.66M) of all BET tokens. Those are dedicated to stimulating the market.

*   The Bonus Pool lies in the vesting contract for 5 years.
    
*   Vesting allows to unlock approx. 2.722B BET tokens a quarter since **1st June 2024**
    
*   The Bonus Pool has no exact purpose of the usage but is designed to be used for project benefit
    
    *   Usage can be welcome bonuses, special affiliate or partner bonuses or liquidity support
        
    *   Usage of the Bonus Pool will be announced.
        
    

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/tokenomy/bet-initial-distribution/bonus-pool#bonus-pool-consensus)

Bonus pool consensus


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Bonus pool is owned by multisig with quorum of 2 out of 3 [Multisignature (multisig) Principle](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/betfin-governance/betfin-governance/multisignature-multisig-principle)

# Partner | BETFIN DOCS

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/core/partner#overview)

Overview

The Partner contract serves as an interface for partners within the ecosystem to interact with betting and staking functionalities. Players can place bets and stake tokens using any of the Partner contracts.

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/core/partner#contract-structure)

Contract Structure

The Partner contract inherits from Ownable, allowing for ownership management. It interacts with the Core contract to access betting and staking functionalities.

#### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/core/partner#constructor)

Constructor

`**constructor**`: Initializes the Partner contract with the specified tariff and owner address.

#### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/core/partner#betting-operations)

Betting Operations

`**placeBet**`: Allows players to place bets.

`**stake**`: Allows players to stake tokens.

#### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/core/partner#withdrawal)

Withdrawal

`**withdraw**`: Allows the owner to withdraw remaining tokens from the contract.

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/core/partner#dependencies)

Dependencies

The Partner contract depends on the Core and Tariff contracts for accessing core functionalities and tariff information within the ecosystem.

[PreviousCore](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/core)
[NextTariff](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/core/tariff)

# Core | BETFIN DOCS

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/core#overview)

Overview


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Core smart contract is the central component of a decentralized application (DApp) ecosystem that manages tariffs, partners, games, stakings, and betting activities. It provides functionalities for creating and managing tariffs, partners, games, and stakings, as well as facilitating betting and staking operations within the ecosystem.

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/core#contract-address)

Contract Address


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The contract is deployed at: [0xBf87898C4e609598a393cCD765482BeF80000000](https://polygonscan.com/address/0xBf87898C4e609598a393cCD765482BeF80000000)

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/core#contract-structure)

Contract Structure


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The contract is structured into different sections corresponding to the management of tariffs, partners, games, stakings, and betting operations.

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/core#tariffs)

Tariffs

`**addTariff**`: Allows the addition of new tariffs with specified pricing, profit, and stake profit parameters.

`**removeTariff**`: Allows the removal of existing tariffs.

`**getTariffs**`: Retrieves a list of all tariffs.

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/core#partners)

Partners

`**addPartner**` Enables partners to register with the system by linking to existing tariffs and making payments.

`getPartners` Retrieves a list of all registered partners.

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/core#games)

Games

`**addGame**`: Permits the addition of new games with version validation.

`**getGames**`: Retrieves a list of all registered games.

`**isGame**`: Checks if a given address corresponds to a registered game.

`**removeGame**`: Allows the removal of existing games.

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/core#stakings)

Stakings

`**addStaking**`: Allows the addition of new stakings with address validation.

`**getStakings**`: Retrieves a list of all registered stakings.

`**isStaking**`: Checks if a given address corresponds to a registered staking.

`**removeStaking**`: Allows the removal of existing stakings.

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/core#betting-operations)

Betting Operations

`**placeBet**`: Enables partners to place bets on behalf of players, with fee calculations and bet creation.

`**stake**`: Enables partners to stake tokens on behalf of players, with profit distribution.

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/core#error-codes)

Error Codes

The contract defines various error codes to indicate specific error conditions encountered during contract execution. These error codes are documented within the contract code and serve as a reference for developers integrating with the contract.

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/core#roles)

Roles

The contract utilizes AccessControl from OpenZeppelin for role-based access control. The roles defined include `PARTNER` and `TIMELOCK`. These roles control access to critical functions within the contract.

[PreviousContracts Overview](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/contracts-overview)
[NextPartner](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/core/partner)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Affiliate Fund | BETFIN DOCS

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/affiliate-contract/affiliate-fund#overview)

Overview

The AffiliateFund smart contract manages the affiliate fund within the application. It facilitates the distribution of bonuses to affiliates based on their activities and conditions set by the affiliate program.

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/affiliate-contract/affiliate-fund#role-based-access-control)

Role-based Access Control

The contract implements role-based access control with two roles: `TIMELOCK` and `SERVICE`. These roles control access to functions responsible for setting affiliate contracts and managing bonuses.

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/affiliate-contract/affiliate-fund#constants)

Constants

*   `DIRECT_STAKING_BONUS`: Percentage of direct staking bonus.
    
*   `DIRECT_BETTING_BONUS`: Percentage of direct betting bonus.
    
*   `MAX_CLAIM_DAILY`: Maximum amount that can be claimed daily.
    
*   `MAX_CLAIM_DAILY_PERCENT`: Maximum percentage of staked amount that can be claimed daily.
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/affiliate-contract/affiliate-fund#events)

Events

*   `MatchingBonusClaimed`: Triggered when a matching bonus is claimed.
    
*   `DirectBonusClaimed`: Triggered when a direct bonus is claimed.
    
*   `NewAffiliate`: Triggered when a new affiliate contract is set.
    
*   `NewMaxClaimDaily`: Triggered when the maximum claim daily value is updated.
    

The Affiliate Fund smart contract manages an affiliate fund within the application. It:

*   Handles the distribution of bonuses to affiliates based on their activities and conditions set by the affiliate program.
    
*   Allows affiliates to claim matching bonuses and direct bonuses.
    
*   Tracks daily claimed bonuses for affiliates to ensure adherence to daily limits.
    
*   Enables the setting of the affiliate contract address and maximum daily claim value.
    

[PreviousAffiliate Contract](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/affiliate-contract)
[NextGame Interface](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/game-interface)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Verify contracts | BETFIN DOCS

Betfin platform is a decentralized technology running on the Polygon blockchain. **Before you connect your wallet, please check if you interact with the Betfin contract otherwise your funds can be lost.**

Steps to Verify:

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/betfin-governance/betfin-contract-addresses/verify-contracts#official-website-and-partners)

**Official Website & partners**

*   The main website for Betfin is [betfin.io](https://betfin.io/)
     which is the only source of truth for Betfin
    
*   As betfin have partner contract option there might be other sites offering interaction with same contracts such as betfin.io
    
*   Here is the official list of Betfin [Partner contracts](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/betfin-governance/betfin-contract-addresses#partner-contracts)
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/betfin-governance/betfin-contract-addresses/verify-contracts#check-contract-address)

**Check Contract Address**

*   Only interact with contracts listed on the official Betfin website or the official partner's page.
    
*   Always verify the contract you are interacting with. That can be done while signing the transaction - the contract must fully match one the partner contracts displayed in the table above. ![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F165088273-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrHOKQrd3to9xOScdSF8N%252Fuploads%252FxzxQxt3W5p2aQncfYIkY%252FScreenshot%25202024-07-13%2520at%252020.48.43.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0fa133e2-bdc2-400d-923c-d47625e1e926&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6966551c&sv=2)
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/betfin-governance/betfin-contract-addresses/verify-contracts#avoid-scams)

*   Never connect your wallet to any website that claims to be Betfin and does not use one of the partner contracts
    
*   **NEVER TRUST ANY THIRD PARTY CONTACTING YOU AS BETFIN SUPPORT.**
    
*   **Never share your private keys or recovery phrase with anyone.**

# Dynamic Staking Pool | BETFIN DOCS

The `DynamicStakingPool` smart contract is a versatile and secure solution for creating dynamic staking pools. This contract utilizes several OpenZeppelin libraries for added security and functionality, including `AccessControl`, `ERC20`, `Math`, and `ReentrancyGuard`.

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/dynamic-staking/dynamic-staking-pool#features)

Features

*   **Dynamic Profit Distribution**: Automatically distributes profits among stakers based on their stake in the pool.
    
*   **Reentrancy Guard**: Protects against reentrancy attacks, ensuring the security of transactions.
    
*   **Access Control**: Implements role-based access control, allowing only authorized addresses to perform certain actions.
    
*   **Event Logging**: Logs significant actions and changes through events for transparency and tracking.
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/dynamic-staking/dynamic-staking-pool#variables)

Variables

*   `duration`: Duration of the staking pool.
    
*   `startCycle`: The start timestamp of the staking cycle.
    
*   `totalStaked`: Total amount of tokens staked in the pool.
    
*   `totalProfit`: Total profit earned by stakers.
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/dynamic-staking/dynamic-staking-pool#functions)

Functions

*   `getStakersCount()`: Returns the number of stakers in the pool.
    
*   `getStake(address staker)`: Returns the stake information for a specific staker.
    
*   `isStaker(address staker)`: Checks if an address is a staker in the pool.
    
*   `isFull()`: Checks if the pool has reached its maximum capacity.
    
*   `getClaimed(address staker)`: Returns the amount of profit claimed by a staker.
    
*   `stake(address staker, uint256 amount)`: Allows an authorized role to add a stake for a staker.
    
*   `withdraw()`: Withdraws staked tokens and distributes profits at the end of the staking cycle.
    
*   `profit(uint256 _profit)`: Records profit to be distributed among stakers.
    
*   `loss(uint256 amount)`: Records a loss, reducing the real stake amount.
    
*   `distributeProfit()`: Distributes profits among stakers based on their stake.
    

[PreviousDynamic Staking](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/dynamic-staking)
[NextPass Contract](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/pass-contract)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Predict Contract | BETFIN DOCS

The `Predict.sol` contract is one of Betfin Games that facilitates prediction games. It is designed to work with other contracts, including `PredictGame` for individual prediction games and `ConservativeStaking` for staking mechanisms. This documentation outlines the key functionalities and components of the `Predict` contract.

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/predict-contract#key-components)

Key Components

#### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/predict-contract#state-variables)

State Variables

*   `core`: An `immutable` reference to the `Core` contract, central to the ecosystem.
    
*   `staking`: An `immutable` reference to the `ConservativeStaking` contract, for staking functionalities.
    
*   `games`: An `address[]` private array holding addresses of all prediction game contracts.
    

#### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/predict-contract#events)

Events

*   `GameCreated(address indexed game)`: Emitted when a new prediction game contract is created.
    
*   `GameDeactivated(address indexed game)`: Emitted when a prediction game contract is deactivated.
    
*   `GameActivated(address indexed game)`: Emitted when a prediction game contract is activated.
    
*   **placeBet (internal)**: Transfers the bet amount to the game contract and calls `placeBet` on the specified `PredictGame`. This is used by the public `placeBet` function after validations.
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/predict-contract#functions)

Functions

*   **addGame**: Creates a new `PredictGame` contract with specified parameters, activates it, and emits `GameCreated`. It performs several checks to ensure valid parameters.
    
*   **deactivate**: Deactivates a specified prediction game contract by calling its `deactivate` function and emits `GameDeactivated`.
    
*   **activate**: Activates a specified prediction game contract by calling its `activate` function and emits `GameActivated`.
    
*   **placeBet**: Places a bet on a specified prediction game. It transfers the bet amount (minus a fee) to the game contract and calls `placeBet` on the specified `PredictGame`.
    

[PreviousBet Interface](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/bet-interface)
[NextPredict Game](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/predict-contract/predict-game)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Affiliate Member | BETFIN DOCS

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/pass-contract/affiliate-member#purpose)

Purpose

`AffiliateMember` is an abstract smart contract that serves as a foundation for managing an affiliate membership system. It leverages OpenZeppelin's `AccessControl` for role-based access control, enabling specific functionalities to be restricted to users with certain roles.

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/pass-contract/affiliate-member#key-features)

Key Features

*   Tracks affiliate members and their relationships (inviters and invitees).
    
*   Manages bonuses for direct staking, direct betting, and matching bonuses.
    

Function

Description

`getInviter`

Returns the inviter of a specific member.

`getInviteesCount`

Returns the number of invitees a member has.

`getMembersCount`

Returns the total count of members.

`getInvitee`

Returns a specific invitee of a member.

`getInvitees`

Returns all invitees of a member.

`claimDirectBettingBonus`, `claimDirectStakingBonus`, `claimMatchingBonus`

Allows claiming of various bonuses for members.

`getClaimedDirectStakingBonus`, `getClaimedDirectBettingBonus`, `getClaimedMatchingBonus`

Returns the amount of bonuses claimed by a member.

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/pass-contract/affiliate-member#events)

Events

*   `NewMember(address indexed member, address indexed inviter, address indexed parent)`

# Affiliate Pool | BETFIN DOCS

The affiliate pool is the biggest part of the initial distribution. It includes 49% of all issued tokens (381.11B BET tokens) and represents the main business engine of the whole project.

*   Those tokens have no vesting but are unlocked by users for affiliation of new stakers or bettors only.
    
*   The only way how affiliate pool can be unlocked is through business acquisition.
    
*   Tokens are held on a special contract called Affiliate fund.
    

**The affiliate pool is used to cover the following (check the affiliate terms)**

*   Direct affiliate bonus of 0,5% from all bets and 7% of all stakes.
    
*   8% weak leg matching bonus which is counted from 100% of all stakes and 1% of all bets
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/tokenomy/bet-initial-distribution/affiliate-pool#relevant-links)

Relevant links

*   See the [Affiliate Contract](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/affiliate-contract)
    
*   Read the affiliate fund contract: [https://polygonscan.com/token/0xbf7970d56a150cd0b60bd08388a4a75a27777777?a=0xbfcdb5b5102f376aefa31129e8125d04b3666666#code](https://polygonscan.com/token/0xbf7970d56a150cd0b60bd08388a4a75a27777777?a=0xbfcdb5b5102f376aefa31129e8125d04b3666666#code)
    
*   Check the [Affiliate Terms](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/affiliate-manual/affiliate-terms)
    

[PreviousAirdrop Pool](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/tokenomy/bet-initial-distribution/airdrop-pool)
[NextBonus Pool](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/tokenomy/bet-initial-distribution/bonus-pool)

Last updated 11 months ago

# Pass Contract | BETFIN DOCS

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/pass-contract#purpose)

Purpose

`Pass` extends from `ERC721` (an OpenZeppelin implementation of the ERC721 standard for NFTs), `AffiliateMember`, and `ReentrancyGuard`. Its main functionality is to mint NFT passes for members of the affiliate system, ensuring unique ownership and adherence to specific conditions set by the affiliate system.

#### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/pass-contract#key-features)

Key Features

*   Minting NFT passes for new members under certain conditions.
    
*   Disabling and enabling minting for an account.
    
*   Enforcing non-transferability of the passes.
    

#### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/pass-contract#functions-summary)

Functions Summary

Function

Access

Description

Constructor

Constructor

Sets up the ERC721 token name, symbol, and admin role.

`mint`

External/NonReentrant

Mints a new pass for a member, ensuring various conditions are met.

`disableMint`, `enableMint`

Public

Allows a member to disable or enable minting for their account.

# Affiliate Contract | BETFIN DOCS

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/affiliate-contract#contract-structure)

Contract Structure

The contract is structured to handle affiliate-related functionalities, including checking conditions, managing bonuses, and setting parameters.

The Affiliate smart contract manages an affiliate program within the application. It:

*   Checks if a member can invite new members based on specific conditions.
    
*   Checks if a member is eligible to receive matching bonuses based on their staking and invitee activities.
    
*   Stores and manages matching bonuses for members.
    
*   Allows authorized users to set various conditions and parameters for the affiliate program.
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/affiliate-contract#role-based-access-control)

Role-based Access Control

The contract implements role-based access control with two roles:

*   `BINAR`: Allows setting matching bonuses.
    
*   `TIMELOCK`: Allows setting various contract parameters.
    

#### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/affiliate-contract#constants)

Constants

*   `TOTAL_MATCHING_PART`: Total matching bonus allocation.
    
*   `BETTING_MATCHING_PART`: Matching bonus allocated for betting.
    
*   `STAKING_MATCHING_PART`: Matching bonus allocated for staking.
    

#### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/affiliate-contract#storage)

Storage

*   `inviteStakingCondition`: Minimum staking condition required for inviting new members.
    
*   `matchingStakingCondition`: Minimum staking condition required for receiving matching bonuses.
    
*   `matchingInviteeCondition`: Minimum staking condition required for invitees to trigger matching bonuses.
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/affiliate-contract#events)

Events

*   `NewMatchingBonus`: Triggered when a new matching bonus is set.
    
*   `NewPass`: Triggered when a new instance of Pass contract is set.
    
*   `NewConservativeStaking`: Triggered when a new instance of ConservativeStaking contract is set.
    
*   `NewDynamicStaking`: Triggered when a new instance of DynamicStaking contract is set.
    
*   `NewBetsMemory`: Triggered when a new instance of BetsMemory contract is set.
    
*   `NewInviteStakingCondition`: Triggered when the invite staking condition is updated.
    
*   `NewMatchingStakingCondition`: Triggered when the matching staking condition is updated.
    
*   `NewMatchingInviteeCondition`: Triggered when the matching invitee condition is updated.
    

[PreviousAffiliate Member](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/pass-contract/affiliate-member)
[NextAffiliate Fund](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/affiliate-contract/affiliate-fund)

# Roulette Bet | BETFIN DOCS

`RouletteBet` is a Solidity smart contract designed for the blockchain-based game of Roulette. It manages individual bets placed by players, tracking various details such as the bet amount, the specific condition or numbers bet on (represented as a bitmap), and the outcome of the bet. This contract is integral to the game's operation, providing functions to set and retrieve bet information, ensuring secure and verified gameplay.

`RouletteBet` inherits from `Ownable` and implements the `BetInterface`, providing a structured approach to managing a roulette bet's lifecycle and data. It encapsulates bet details, including the player's address, the associated game, amounts, and outcomes, with access control enforced through the `Ownable` contract.

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/roulette/roulette-bet#usage-scenario)

Usage Scenario

In a typical usage scenario, a `Roulette` game contract will instantiate a `RouletteBet` for each bet made by a player. The game contract, acting as the owner of the bet contract, will then update the bet details based on game outcomes, such as determining whether the player wins or loses and updating the bet status and result accordingly.

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/roulette/roulette-bet#functions)

**Functions**

*   **Getters**: Functions to retrieve bet information, such as `getPlayer()`, `getGame()`, `getAmount()`, `getStatus()`, `getCreated()`, `getResult()`, `getBetInfo()`, `getRequestId()`, `getWinNumber()`, `getBetsCount()`, and `getBet(index)`.
    
*   **Setters**: Functions to set bet details, restricted to the contract owner (e.g., `setPlayer()`, `setGame()`, `setAmount()`, `setStatus()`, `setRequestId()`, `setResult()`, `setWinNumber()`, `setBets()`).
    

[PreviousRoulette](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/roulette)
[NextError Codes](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/error-codes)

# General FAQ | BETFIN DOCS

Who owns and operates the Betfin?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/betfin-governance/general-faq#who-owns-and-operates-the-betfin)

Betfin is not owned or operated by any single entity as it is an autonomous web3 application that is being developed, operated and promoted by the Betfin community.

*   All decisions are being made based on [Betfin governance](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/betfin-governance/betfin-governance)
    
*   All revenues from Betfin are distributed among staking users so there is no single owner of the project.
    

Can I speak to someone from Betfin?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/betfin-governance/general-faq#can-i-speak-to-someone-from-betfin)

*   You can reach the community via discussion in Github -
    
    *   See the inke here: [https://github.com/orgs/betfinio/discussions](https://github.com/orgs/betfinio/discussions)
        
    
*   You can also use the chat on any of the website in betfin ecosystem
    
    *   Remember that if anyone contacts you as Betfin support, it is not true!
        
    

Can I join the Betfin team?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/betfin-governance/general-faq#can-i-join-the-betfin-team)

Yes, anyone from the Betfin community can participate in the project. Reach the Betfin support or github discussion with your abilities.

*   Do not spam any public group with your offers
    

Is the project legal and what is its legal status?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/betfin-governance/general-faq#is-the-project-legal-and-what-is-its-legal-status)

From the legal point of view, Betfin is a public platform that allows community members to use smart contracts with pre-defined functions and rules. Therefore there is no relation between the user and Betfin but only a relationship between users through public Betfin smartcontracts.

It is your sole responsibility to find out whether participation in such contracts is legal.

Is there KYC on Betfin?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/betfin-governance/general-faq#is-there-kyc-on-betfin)

Betfin does not enforce any KYC but it is possible that certain partner in Betfin ecosystem would require standard KYC process according to the local regulations. Betfin itself is decentralized application that has no option how to enforce KYC or even store users personal data.

Can Betfin freeze or misuse my funds?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/betfin-governance/general-faq#can-betfin-freeze-or-misuse-my-funds)

No, as no one has control of the contract execution and moreover it is technically impossible as the contract is autonomous.

Am I anonymous while using Betfin?[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/betfin-governance/general-faq#am-i-anonymous-while-using-betfin)

You are anonymous until someone connects your identity with your wallet ID. All your transaction are publicly available data.

This rule applies to the whole crypto space.

[PreviousInternal Wallets & External Contracts](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/betfin-governance/internal-wallets-and-external-contracts)
[NextContracts Overview](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/contracts-overview)

Last updated 9 months ago

# Conservative Staking | BETFIN DOCS

ConservativeStaking is a smart contract intended for staking purposes within a blockchain ecosystem. It integrates with other contracts such as `ConservativeStakingPool` and utilises `Pass` for additional functionalities. This contract is designed to offer a conservative staking mechanism, allowing users to stake tokens, claim profits, and participate in a structured reward distribution system.

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/conservative-staking#features)

Features

*   **Staking**: Users can stake tokens in different pools.
    
*   **Profit Calculation and Distribution**: Calculates profit based on staked amounts and distributes it accordingly.
    
*   **Claiming**: Users can claim their profits from individual pools or all at once.
    
*   **Conservative Pool Management**: Supports opening new pools and closing existing ones based on specific conditions.
    

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/conservative-staking#contract-structure)

Contract Structure

Element

Description

**Variables**

\- Stores contract state such as pools, staked amounts, profits, and roles.

**Events**

\- Signals significant actions in the contract like pool openings/closings, staking, claiming, etc.

**Public Functions**

\- Functions accessible to all users for actions like staking, claiming, and viewing contract data.

**External Functions**

\- Functions callable from other contracts, mainly for administrative purposes.

**Internal Functions**

\- Utility functions for internal contract management, not accessible externally.

### 

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/smartcontracts-description/conservative-staking#functions)

Functions

View Functions

User functions

Administrative functions

Function name

Description

`getStaked(address staker)`

Returns the amount staked by a specific user.

`totalClaimed()`

Returns the total amount of tokens claimed by all users

`totalStaked()`

Returns the total amount of tokens staked in the contract

`totalProfit()`

Returns the total profit generated by the contract

`totalStakers()`

Returns the total number of users who have staked tokens

`getActivePoolCount()`, `getStakedPoolsCount(address staker)`, `getProfit(address staker)`, `getClaimable(address staker)`

Provide detailed information about pools and profits.

Function name

Description

`stake(address staker, uint256 amount)`

Allows a user to stake a specified amount of tokens.

`claim(address pool)`, `claimAll()`

Allows users to claim profits from specific or all pools.

`withdraw(address pool)`

Allows users to withdraw their staked amount from a specific pool.

Function name

Description

`setCalculatingWindow(uint256 _window)`

Adjusts the calculation window for profit distribution

`setMinAllowedAmount(uint256 _amount)`

Sets the minimum amount of tokens that can be staked.

`newPool()`

Manually triggers the creation of a new staking pool.

The `ConservativeStaking` contract provides a comprehensive solution for staking mechanisms, emphasizing security with its non-reentrancy guard and flexibility through dynamic pool management

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/audits-and-bug-bounty/report-an-issue#step-1)

Step 1.


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Go to: [https://github.com/orgs/betfinio/discussions](https://github.com/orgs/betfinio/discussions)

Please check the list of already reported issues to avoid reporting one and the same thing twice.

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/audits-and-bug-bounty/report-an-issue#step-2)

Step 2.


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click on "New discussion".

![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F165088273-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrHOKQrd3to9xOScdSF8N%252Fuploads%252FCw7P4saPUvzxOJaMaccd%252FScreenshot%25202024-11-21%2520at%252013.52.34.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D841415ee-182f-4aa3-85a8-54838b094754&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e15cf779&sv=2)

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/audits-and-bug-bounty/report-an-issue#step-3)

Step 3.


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Find "Bugs & Reports" and click "Get started".

![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F165088273-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrHOKQrd3to9xOScdSF8N%252Fuploads%252FjzsLxRuMwuohM9HCTMEc%252FScreenshot%25202024-11-21%2520at%252013.53.40.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0638ac59-d771-4042-b949-68dbcad86b94&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c9c1a82&sv=2)

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/audits-and-bug-bounty/report-an-issue#step-4)

Step 4.


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Type in a title that will help us understand what is the issue about
    
2.  Describe the issue (add links if possible)
    
3.  Add screenshot if possible
    
4.  Click on "Start discussion"
    

![](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F165088273-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FrHOKQrd3to9xOScdSF8N%252Fuploads%252FGOvwyoo3Z8ovDeymQiFy%252FScreenshot%25202024-11-21%2520at%252013.55.32.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D840285bc-12cc-4a25-a9a4-80bd772eac38&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8096946c&sv=2)

[](https://betfin.gitbook.io/betfin-public/audits-and-bug-bounty/report-an-issue#thats-it)

That's it!


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

A member of our team will take it from here. Thank you for helping to improve the experience for everyone using Betfin!
